)@@G@@O  0,X11 .       -> ENTER USER CODE @I@@@@/ . --------------------------JK
)@@G@@--------------------------------------------------    @E@@@@ . *** EXECUJL
)@@G@@TION CONTROL:  AGGREGATE STORAGE ALLOCATOR ***  @I@@@@ . ---------------JM
)@@G@@--------------------------------------------------------------    @C@@@@JN
)@@G@@ . THE ROUTINE IS CALLED BY THE BLOCK/PROCEDURE @F@@@@ . PROLOGUE ROUTINJO
)@@G@@E AND THE AGGREGATE TEMPORARY ALLOCATOR,EXTMP1. @]@@@@ . INPUT:   @H@@@@JP
)@@G@@ .       X1              = A(DV) OF DATA ITEM FOR WHICH STORAGE IS TO BEJQ
)@@G@@ ALL  @D@@@@ .       X4              = A(SD) OF THIS SAME ITEM    @E@@@@JR
)@@G@@ .                           INCREMENTOR MUST CONTAIN ZERO  @]@@@@ . ACTJS
)@@G@@ION:  @F@@@@ .       SPACE IS ACQUIRED ON THE MAIN STACK TO ACCOMODATE TJT
)@@G@@HE    @E@@@@ . DATA ITEM.  IF THE ITEM IS AN ARRAY, ITS DOPE VECTOR IS  JU
)@@G@@@F@@@@ . COMPLETED BY ADDING THE MULTIPLIERS (EXTEN T - 1 AND LOWER     JV
)@@G@@@E@@@@ . BOUNDS SHOULD BE IN HALF WORD FORMAT).  FOR ARRAYS OF    @G@@@@JW
)@@G@@ . STRINGS, SECONDARY DOPE VECTORS ARE ALSO ALLOCATED AND INITIALIZED.  JX
)@@G@@@]@@@@ . RETURN:  @A@@@@ .       X1    A(DV) OF DATA ITEMS  @F@@@@ .    JY
)@@G@@   X4              =A(SD) OF DATA ITEM(UNCHANGED FROM INPUT)@E@@@@ . DESJZ
)@@G@@TROYS:  REGISTERS X2, X3, X5, A1 TO A7, A9 TO A14     @ @@@@ . INTERNAL KA
)@@G@@REGISTER USAGE:   @D@@@@ .       X2              = BASE OF AREA TO BE CLKB
)@@G@@EARED @D@@@@ .       A2              = FIRST WORD BEYOND AREA     @E@@@@KC
)@@G@@ .       R1              = LENGTH OF AREA TO BE CLEARED     @F@@@@ .    KD
)@@G@@   A3                  = ADDRESS OF INITIALIZATION CONSTANT @G@@@@ .    KE
)@@G@@   A5-A6               = F REGISTER (PACKED SDCLS1 AND SDCLS2)    @A@@@@KF
)@@G@@ .       X4              = A(SD)    @E@@@@ .       X1              = A(DKG
)@@G@@V)   (ZERO IN INCREMENTOR)    @C@@@@ .       A12                 = BYTE KH
)@@G@@POINTER     @F@@@@ .       A9-A10              =1ST WORD OF STRING DOPE KI
)@@G@@VECTORS     @F@@@@ .       A11                 = 2ND WORD OF STRING DOPEKJ

)@@G@@H FIELD     @G@@@@         SLB   A11,18 .      LEFT JUSTIFY TO SET CURRELF
)@@G@@NT LENGTH = 0     @G@@@@EXALL4   LABEL .             MERGE TO COMPLETE SLG

)@@G@@ TO DIVIDE BY RIGHT JUSTIFYING MAX LENGTH @F@@@@         SRB     A2,34 .LJ

)@@G@@ITIALIZE    @[@@@@.     @F@@@@. SEE IF IT IS PTR AND IF SO ZERO IT OUT AMB
)@@G@@ND LINK THEM TOGETHER   @[@@@@.     @D@@@@         SRB     A5,18 .      MC

)@@G@@D    A3,GENPAT,X10 .   PUT PTR AT FRONT OF LIST @A@@@@         STORE   XMN
)@@G@@5,GENPAT,X10 .    @E@@@@         STORE   A3,W1H2+2,*X5 . MOVE TO NEXT PTMO
)@@G@@R IN ARRAY  @E@@@@         IF A2,GT,X5 THEN,EXAL11 . -> IF END NOT REACHMP
)@@G@@ED    @#@@@@         JMP .    @[@@@@.     @[@@@@.     @#@@@@EXAL10   LABMQ
)@@G@@EL .  @E@@@@         GOTO  EXCLR .       -> INITIALIZE SCALER AND RETURNMR
)@@G@@@C@@@@EXALL5   LABEL .              STRING ARRAYS     @H@@@@         LOAMS
)@@G@@D  A4,2,I .      ARRAY MEMBERS ARE SECONDARY DOPE VECTORS(LEN=2)  @G@@@@MT
)@@G@@         LOADXI X2,2,I .     SET INCREMENTOR FOR DOPE VECTOR POINTER    MU
)@@G@@@G@@@@EXALL6   LABEL .             MERGE TO INITIALIZE DOPE VECTOR POINTMV

)@@G@@DIMENSIONS  @D@@@@         ADD   X3,W1XU,X3 .  DOUBLE DIMENSION COUNT   MX
)@@G@@@H@@@@         ADD   X3,W1XU,X1 .  POINT TO LAST MULTIPLIER SLOT IN DOPEMY
)@@G@@ VECTOR     @G@@@@         LOADXI X3,-2,I .    SET TO DECREMENT DOPE VECMZ
)@@G@@TOR MPLR POINTER  @E@@@@         LOAD  A7,W1XU,X2 .  INITIALIZE VIRTUAL NA
)@@G@@ORIGIN SUM  @F@@@@         LOAD  A13,1,I .     SET CONSTANT FOR EXTENT CNB
)@@G@@ALCULATIONS @C@@@@ . ** FORM MULTIPLIERS AND VIRTUAL ORIGIN **    @F@@@@NC
)@@G@@EXALL7   LABEL .             TOP OF LOOP, COMPUTE VIRUAL ORIGIN   @G@@@@ND
)@@G@@         STORE A4,W1,X3 .    SET MULTIPLIER INTO MAIN DOPE VECTOR (M(I))NE
)@@G@@@D@@@@         LOAD  A8,W1XH2+1,X3 . I-TH LOWER BOUND (L(I))@C@@@@      NF
)@@G@@   MPYS  A8,A4 .       A8 = M(I) * L(I)   @H@@@@         SUB   A7,A8 .  NG
)@@G@@     FORM VIRTUAL ORIGIN = SUM(-M(I)*L(I))+REAL ORIGIN@E@@@@EXALL8   LABNH
)@@G@@EL .             COMPUTE AND TEST MULTIPLIER    @F@@@@         AU,H1 A13NI
)@@G@@,1,*X3 .   A14 = EXTENT(I)               *******@F@@@@         MPYS  A4,NJ
)@@G@@A14 .      COMPUTE MULTIPLIER M(I) * EXTENT (I) @F@@@@         IF    A4,NK
)@@G@@GE,KEXTNT,I THEN,EXMPOV . -> MULTIPLIER OVERFLOW@G@@@@         TLEM,XU XNL
)@@G@@1,0,X3 .   I := I - 1, M(I) := M(I+1) * EXTENT(I+1)   @C@@@@         GOTNM
)@@G@@O  EXALL7 .      -> MORE DIMENSIONS @F@@@@ . ** SET VIRTUAL ORIGIN IN DONN
)@@G@@PE VECTOR AND INITIALIZE ARRAY **   @F@@@@         STORE A7,ARDVOR,X1 . NO
)@@G@@         IMPLANT VIRTUAL ORIGIN     @I@@@@         IF    SDARST*01000,OFNP
)@@G@@F THEN,EXALL9 . -> FINISH NON-STRING ARRAY INITIAL    @C@@@@ . ** ALLOCANQ
)@@G@@TE SECONDARY STRING DOPE VECTORS ** @H@@@@         ADD   A4,W1XU,X2 .  FNR
)@@G@@IRST FREE WORD BEYOND SECONDARY DOPE VECTORS    @D@@@@EXALS3   LABEL .  NS
)@@G@@                 TRY TO FIND STORAGE@G@@@@         IF    A4,LT,ADPCND THNT
)@@G@@EN,EXALS2 . -> STORAGE CAPACITY EXCEEDED? @D@@@@         LOCAL .        NU
)@@G@@           SAVE RETURN ADDRESS@D@@@@         LINK    WROVFL .          GNV
)@@G@@ET MORE STORAGE   @G@@@@         UNSTK   X11 .             RECLAIM RETURNW
)@@G@@N ADDRESS FROM STACK    @E@@@@         GOTO    EXALS3 .          GO BACKNX
)@@G@@ AND TRY AGAIN    @E@@@@EXALS2   LABEL .                   HERE WITH ENONY
)@@G@@UGH STORAGE @H@@@@         AU    A9,A4 .       A10 = FIRST WORD OF 1ST SNZ
)@@G@@ECONDARY DOPE VECTOR    @F@@@@EXALS1   LABEL .             INITIALIZE A OA
)@@G@@SECONDARY DOPE VECTOR   @F@@@@         STORE A10,ARDVOR,X2 .         SETOB
)@@G@@ FLAGS AND WORD POINTER @F@@@@         STORE A11,ARDVSZ,X2 .         ESTOC
)@@G@@ABLISH LENGTH FIELDS    @D@@@@         ADD   A10,A1 .      ADD IN WHOLE OD
)@@G@@WORDS USED  @H@@@@         TG,U    A4,3,*X2 .    HAS LAST SECONDARY DOPEOE

)@@G@@@A@@@@ . EXPRESSION IS BEING EVALUATED.   @]@@@@ . ACTION:  @G@@@@ .    PI
)@@G@@   IF THE N-TH BIT OF THE SELECTOR BITS WORD (SBW) IS SET THEN THE@D@@@@PJ

)@@G@@ .    @D@@@@         IF    SDBROT,ZERO THEN,EXTP21 . -> NO BROTHER@F@@@@XH
)@@G@@         LSDP  X4,SDBROT,X4 .          TEST BROTHER FOR SON, ETC  @^@@@@XI
)@@G@@         GOTO  EXTP11 . @#@@@@EXTP21   LABEL .  @D@@@@         LSDP  X4,XJ
)@@G@@SDDAD,X4 . FOLLOW FATHER'S POINTER  @E@@@@         GOTO  EXTP06 .      -XK
)@@G@@> TEST FATHER FOR BROTHER, ETC@B@@@@EXTP07   LABEL .             FINISH XL
)@@G@@UP    @E@@@@         LOAD  A1,W1XU,X7 .  RETURN ADDRESS OF TEMPORARY DV XM
)@@G@@@C@@@@         LMJ   X5,EXML .     RESTORE REGISTERS  @F@@@@         GOTXN
)@@G@@O  2,X11 .       RETURN USING SAVED ADDRESS FROM AR   @I@@@@/ . --------XO
)@@G@@--------------------------------------------------------------------    XP
)@@G@@@E@@@@ . *** EXECUTION CONTROL:  VARAIBLE DATA AREA MANAGEMENT ***@I@@@@XQ
)@@G@@ . ---------------------------------------------------------------------XR
)@@G@@--------    @A@@@@ . OBTAIN NEW VARIABLE DATA AREA    @ @@@@         USIXS
)@@G@@NG AREC,X10 .     @E@@@@EXGDVA*  LLOC .              ENTRY POINT FROM USXT
)@@G@@ER CODE     @H@@@@         LOAD  A1,AREPTR,X10 .         END OF CURRENT XU
)@@G@@VARIABLE DATA AREA (VDA)@F@@@@         LOAD  R1,ARVDAP,X10 .         SAVXV
)@@G@@E END OF PREVIOUS VDA   @C@@@@         STORE R1,W1,A1 .   IN NEXT FREE WXW
)@@G@@ORD   @H@@@@         STORE A1,ARVDAP,X10 .         VDA POINTER POINTS TOXX
)@@G@@ THAT POINTER     @E@@@@         ADD   A1,1,I . NEW VDA STARTS JUST BEYOXY
)@@G@@ND POINTER  @G@@@@         STORE A1,AREPTR,X10 .         END PTR POINTS XZ
)@@G@@TO FIRST FREE WORD@C@@@@         LJMP .              -> RETURN TO CALLERYA
)@@G@@@H@@@@/ . --------------------------------------------------------------YB
)@@G@@------------@E@@@@ . CALLED BY CODE FOR SOURCE "STOP" OR "EXIT" STATEMENYC
)@@G@@T     @H@@@@ . ---------------------------------------------------------YD
)@@G@@------------------@#@@@@EXSTOP*  LABEL .  @F@@@@         STORE   R11,ARSYE
)@@G@@TMT .      SET STATEMENT NUMBER FOR PMD   @^@@@@ . 'PROGRAM IS STOPPED.'YF
)@@G@@@G@@@@   ONUNIT  EREXSTOP,ACCDFN,0,I  PLEXND,PLEXND,PLEXND  DEXWK1,0  DEYG
)@@G@@XMAX,0@C@@@@ . ** ROUTINE TO HANDLE IMPROPER STRING LENGTHS @B@@@@EXTMSLYH
)@@G@@   LOCAL .             ENTRY POINT  @ @@@@         ONER EREXTMSL,2 .    YI
)@@G@@@G@@@@ . 'STRING LENGTH ', NUMA5, ' OF ',SDX4, ' IS IMPROPER.  80 IS USEYJ
)@@G@@D.'   @D@@@@         LOAD  A5,80,I .     CORRECTION STRING LENGTH @C@@@@YK
)@@G@@         JMP .               -> RETURN TO CALLER@I@@@@/. ---------------YL
)@@G@@--------------------------------------------------------------    @C@@@@YM
)@@G@@ . ** PREPARE MULTIPLE SUBSCRIPT LIST ENTRIES **@I@@@@ . ---------------YN
)@@G@@--------------------------------------------------------------    @F@@@@YO
)@@G@@ . ADDS A LIST OF TALLY CELL INDICIES TO A LIST OF LOWER BOUNDS   @C@@@@YP
)@@G@@ . TO PRODUCE A LIST OF FULLWORD SUBSCRIPTS     @]@@@@ . INPUT:   @A@@@@YQ
)@@G@@ .       A1 = A(TALLY CELL INDEX)   @A@@@@ .       A2 = A(NEXT LOWER BOUYR
)@@G@@ND)   @B@@@@ .       A3 = A(NEXT SUBSCRIPT LIST SLOT) @E@@@@ .       R1 YS
)@@G@@= LOOP COUNT = NUMBER OF CONSECUTIVE STARS - 1  @A@@@@ . DESTROYS:  A1, YT
)@@G@@A2, A3, AND R1    @B@@@@EXPMSL*  LLOC .              ENTRY POINT  @D@@@@YU
)@@G@@         LOADXI A1,1,I .     TALLY CELL INCREMENTOR   @D@@@@         LOAYV
)@@G@@DXI A2,2,I .     DOPE VECTOR INCREMENTOR  @E@@@@         LOADXI A3,1,I .YW
)@@G@@     SUBSCRIPT LIST INCREMENTOR     @#@@@@EXPMS1   LABEL .  @E@@@@      YX
)@@G@@   LOAD  A4,W1XH2,*A1 .          TALLY CELL OFFSET    @H@@@@         ADDYY
)@@G@@   A4,W1XH2,*A2 .          TRUE SUBSCRIPT VALUE FROM LOWER BOUND  @D@@@@YZ
)@@G@@         STORE A4,W1,*A3 .   PUT IN SUBSCRIPT LIST    @D@@@@         LOOZA
)@@G@@P  R1,EXPMS1 .   -> MORE STAR SUBSCRIPTS  @D@@@@         LJMP .         ZB
)@@G@@     -> RETURN TO USER CODE   @I@@@@ . ---------------------------------ZC
)@@G@@--------------------------------------------    @D@@@@ . ** USER CODE COZD
)@@G@@RRECTION FOR NEGATIVE EXTENT - 1    @I@@@@ . ---------------------------ZE
)@@G@@--------------------------------------------------    @H@@@@EXJGDE*  LOCZF
)@@G@@AL .             EXTENT - 1 WAS COMPUTED NEGATIVE IN USER CODE    @E@@@@ZG
)@@G@@         SUB   X11,2,I .     GET ADDRESS OF JGD BEFORE LINK @G@@@@      ZH
)@@G@@   LOAD  A3,W1Q2,X11 . GET REGISTER ADDRESS CONTAINING EXTENT - 1 @E@@@@ZI
)@@G@@         SRB   A3,4 .        RIGHT JUSTIFY REGISTER ADDRESS @C@@@@      ZJ
)@@G@@   LOAD  A4,W1,A3 .    IMPROPER EXTENT - 1@D@@@@         ADD   A4,1,I . ZK
)@@G@@     COMPUTE IMPROPER EXTENT  @F@@@@         ONUNIT  EREXJGDE,ACCDSU,2  ZL
)@@G@@R,I,R  DEXWK1,4  DEXMAX,4     @C@@@@.        USE LOWER BOUND : LOWERBOUNZM
)@@G@@D + 10 .    @H@@@@ . 'UPPER BOUND', NUMA4, 'WAS LESS THAN LOWER BOUND OFZN
)@@G@@ 1.  (1:10) IS USED.'   @D@@@@         LOAD  A4,9,I .      SET REPAIRED ZO
)@@G@@EXTENT - 1  @C@@@@         STORE A4,W1,A3 .    REPLACE IN REGISTER@B@@@@ZP
)@@G@@         JMP . -> RETURN TO USER CODE     @I@@@@/. ---------------------ZQ
)@@G@@--------------------------------------------------------    @B@@@@ . ** ZR
)@@G@@FIXED BINARY HALFWORD OVERFLOW **   @I@@@@ . ---------------------------ZS
)@@G@@--------------------------------------------------    @D@@@@ . CALLED BYZT
)@@G@@ USER CODE WHEN VALUE IS TOO LARGE TO     @C@@@@ . FITTED INTO A FIXED BZU
)@@G@@INARY HALFWORD (17,0).  @F@@@@ . A CORRECTION IS MADE TO THE REGISTER COZV
)@@G@@NTAINING THE OPERAND    @C@@@@EXHWOV*  LOCAL .             SAVE RETURN AZW
)@@G@@DDRESS@G@@@@         SUB   X11,2,I .     GET REGISTER NUMBER FROM TG,U AZX
)@@G@@,0400000    @E@@@@         LOAD  A3,W1Q2,X11 . REGISTER  NUMBER WITH SHIZY
)@@G@@FT    @E@@@@         SRB   A3,4 .        RIGHT JUSTIFY REGISTER NUMBER  ZZ
)@@G@@@D@@@@         LOAD  A4,W1+A0,A3 . FETCH INCORRECT VALUE    @F@@@@      AA
)@@G@@   ONUNIT  EREXHWOV,ACCDSI,2  R,I,JMP  DEXWK1,4  DEXMAX,4   @E@@@@ . 'LEAB
)@@G@@NGTH OR BOUND', NUMA4, ' IS TOO LARGE.  10 IS USED.'  @D@@@@         LOAAC
)@@G@@D  A4,10,I .     USE CORRECTION OF 10     @E@@@@         STORE A4,W1+A0,AD
)@@G@@A3 . SET CORRECTION INTO REGISTER   @C@@@@         JMP . -> RETURN TO CAAE
)@@G@@LLER IN USER CODE @D@@@@EXMST*   LLOC .              RETURN ADDRESS IN XAF
)@@G@@5     @F@@@@         STORE R11,ARSTMT,X10 .         SAVE STATEMENT NUMBEAG
)@@G@@R     @G@@@@         STORE X11,ARSV11,X10 .        SAVE MODIFIERS OF BASAH
)@@G@@E REGISTERS @ @@@@         STORE X7,ARSVX7,X10 .@ @@@@         STORE X8,AI
)@@G@@ARSVX8,X10 .@ @@@@         STORE X9,ARSVX9,X10 .@F@@@@         STORED A5AJ
)@@G@@,ARSVA5,X10 .        SAVE 'A' REGISTER PAIRS    @A@@@@         STORED A7AK
)@@G@@,ARSVA7,X10 .     @A@@@@         STORED A9,ARSVA9,X10 .     @A@@@@      AL
)@@G@@   STORED A11,ARSA11,X10 .    @A@@@@         STORED A13,ARSA13,X10 .    AM
)@@G@@@A@@@@         STORED A15,ARSA15,X10 .    @E@@@@         STORE X1,ARSAX1AN
)@@G@@,X10 .         SAVE I/O REGISTERS   @ @@@@         STORE X2,ARSAX2,X10 .AO
)@@G@@@ @@@@         STORE X3,ARSAX3,X10 .@F@@@@         STORE   X6,ARSVX6,X10AP
)@@G@@ .    SAVE MANAGED 'X' REGISTERS    @A@@@@         STORE   X4,ARSVX4,X10AQ
)@@G@@ .    @C@@@@         GOTO  0,X5 .        ->RETURN TO CALLER @D@@@@EXML* AR
)@@G@@   LLOC .              RETURN ADDRESS IN X5     @F@@@@         LOAD  R11AS
)@@G@@,ARSTMT,X10 .         RESTORE STATEMENT NUMBER  @H@@@@         LOADXM X1AT
)@@G@@1,ARSV11,X10 .       RESTORE MODIFIERS OF BASE REGISTERS    @A@@@@      AU
)@@G@@   LOADXM X7,ARSVX7,X10 .     @A@@@@         LOADXM X8,ARSVX8,X10 .     AV
)@@G@@@A@@@@         LOADXM X9,ARSVX9,X10 .     @F@@@@         LOADD A5,ARSVA5AW
)@@G@@,X10 .         RESTORE 'A' REGISTER PAIRS @ @@@@         LOADD A7,ARSVA7AX
)@@G@@,X10 .@ @@@@         LOADD A9,ARSVA9,X10 .@A@@@@         LOADD A11,ARSA1AY
)@@G@@1,X10 .     @A@@@@         LOADD A13,ARSA13,X10 .     @A@@@@         LOAAZ
)@@G@@DD A15,ARSA15,X10 .     @E@@@@         LOAD  X1,ARSAX1,X10 .         RELBA
)@@G@@OAD I/O REGISTERS @ @@@@         LOAD  X2,ARSAX2,X10 .@ @@@@         LOABB
)@@G@@D  X3,ARSAX3,X10 .@F@@@@         LOAD    X6,ARSVX6,X10 .   RELOAD MANAGEBC
)@@G@@D 'X' REGISTERS   @A@@@@         LOAD    X4,ARSVX4,X10 .    @C@@@@      BD
)@@G@@   GOTO  0,X5 .        -> RETURN TO CALLER@D@@@@EXSAVE*  LLOC .         BE
)@@G@@     RETURN ADDRESS IN X5     @ @@@@         STORE X1,DEXSVE .    @ @@@@BF
)@@G@@         STORE X2,DEXSVE+1 .  @ @@@@         STORE X3,DEXSVE+2 .  @ @@@@BG
)@@G@@         STORED A5,DEXSVE+3 . @E@@@@         STORE   X4,DEXSVE+5 .     SBH
)@@G@@AVE MANAGED 'X' REG     @^@@@@         GOTO  0,X5 .   @D@@@@EXUNSV*  LLOBI
)@@G@@C .              RETURN ADDRESS IN X11    @ @@@@         LOAD  X1,DEXSVEBJ
)@@G@@ .    @ @@@@         LOAD  X2,DEXSVE+1 .  @ @@@@         LOAD  X3,DEXSVEBK
)@@G@@+2 .  @ @@@@         LOADD A5,DEXSVE+3 .  @F@@@@         LOAD    X4,DEXSBL
)@@G@@VE+5 .     RELOAD MANAGED 'X' REGISTER    @#@@@@         LJMP .   @I@@@@BM
)@@G@@/ . --------------------------------------------------------------------BN
)@@G@@--------    @A@@@@ . *** CROSS SECTION COMPUTER ***   @ @@@@ . CALLED BYBO
)@@G@@ COMPILIED CODE   @C@@@@ . A1  = ADDRESS OF LIST OF FULLWORD SUBSCRIPTS BP
)@@G@@@E@@@@ . A2  = ADDRESS OF DOPE VECTOR FROM WHICH CROSS SECTION    @A@@@@BQ
)@@G@@ .            IS TO BE COMPUTED     @F@@@@ . X11 --->             W     BR
)@@G@@     (FLAG BITS) SELECTOR BITS WORD @D@@@@ .                           HBS
)@@G@@1        (SD POINTER)   @H@@@@ .                           XH2       (NUBT
)@@G@@M OF DIM - 1) FOR COMPATIBILITY     @C@@@@ .                           (BU
)@@G@@RETURN POINT)     @E@@@@ . NOTE:  IN FLAG BIT WORD, BIT N IS ON IF SUBSCBV
)@@G@@RIPT N + 1  @B@@@@ .       IN SUPPLIED LIST IS NON-STAR     @]@@@@ . ACTBW
)@@G@@ION:  @F@@@@ .       CREATES A DOPE VECTOR WHICH MAY BE USED TO REFERENCBX
)@@G@@E     @F@@@@ . THE DESIGNATED CROSS-SECTION IN THE SAME MANNER AS FULL ABY
)@@G@@RRAYS @]@@@@ . RETURN:  @E@@@@ .       A1             = ADDRESS OF CREATBZ
)@@G@@ED DOPE VECTOR    @ @@@@ . INTERNAL REGISTER USAGE:   @F@@@@ .       X1 CA
)@@G@@ (A1)       -> LIST OF SUBSCRIPTS (1 IN INCREMENTOR)  @F@@@@ .       X2 CB
)@@G@@ (A2)       -> ORIGINAL DV        (2 IN INCREMENTOR)  @E@@@@ .       X3 CC
)@@G@@                       NUMBER OF DIMENSIONS     @E@@@@ .       X5       CD
)@@G@@                 SAVES CURRENT DV POINTER @C@@@@ .       A1             CE
)@@G@@           SD POINTER   @H@@@@ .       A2                        POINTS CF
)@@G@@TO CREATED SD     (2 IN INCREMENTO  @H@@@@ .       A3                   CG
)@@G@@     SCRATCH CALCULATIONS, LOWER AND UPPER BOU  @D@@@@ .       A4       CH
)@@G@@                 SCRATCH, MULTIPLIER@F@@@@ .       A5                   CI
)@@G@@     VIRTUAL ORIGIN ACCUMULATION    @E@@@@ .       A6                   CJ
)@@G@@     SELECTOR BITS WORD (SBW) @I@@@@ . ---------------------------------CK
)@@G@@--------------------------------------------    @D@@@@EXCRSC*  LOCAL .  CL
)@@G@@           ENTRY FROM COMPILED CODE @D@@@@         LMJ   X5,EXSAVE .   SCM
)@@G@@AVE WORKSPACE REGISTERS @F@@@@         LOADXI A1,1,I .     SET TO ADVANCCN
)@@G@@E SUBSCRIPT LIST POINTER@G@@@@         LOADXI A2,2,I .     SET TO ADVANCCO
)@@G@@E ORIGINAL DOPE VECTOR POINTER@E@@@@         STORED A1,X1 .      CLEAR ACP
)@@G@@1, A2 FOR OTHER PURPOSES@D@@@@         LOAD  A6,W1,X11 .   SBW = SELECTOCQ
)@@G@@R BITS WORD @B@@@@         STORE A6,DEXWK3 .   SAVE SBW     @E@@@@      CR
)@@G@@   LOAD  R1,W1XH2+1,X11 .        GET NUM OF DIMS - 1  @F@@@@         LOACS
)@@G@@D  A1,W1H1+1,X11 .         SD POINTER TO ARGUMENT     @D@@@@         STOCT
)@@G@@RE A1,DEXWK1 .   SAVE FOR LATER COMPARISON@G@@@@         LOADXM A2,AREPTCU
)@@G@@R,X10 .        FIRST AVAILABLE WORD ON STACK    @D@@@@         STORE A2,CV
)@@G@@DEXWK2 .   SAVE TO LOAD A1 AT END   @G@@@@EXCRS1   LABEL .             FCW
)@@G@@OLLOW POINTERS THROUGH SD'S OF STRUCTURE  @C@@@@         USING SDSECT,A1CX
)@@G@@ .   TO BASIC ELEMENTS  @G@@@@         IF    SDSTRU,OFF,SDCLS4 THEN,EXCRCY
)@@G@@S2 . -> BASE ELEMENT FOUND    @D@@@@         LOAD  A1,SDSON,A1 . FOLLOW CZ
)@@G@@SD POINTER TO SON @C@@@@         GOTO  EXCRS1 .      ->CHECK THE SON    DA
)@@G@@@G@@@@EXCRS2   LABEL .             CONSTRUCT DOPE VECTOR FOR CROSS SECTIDB
)@@G@@ON    @C@@@@ .                           OF THIS BASE ARRAY @A@@@@      DC
)@@G@@   LOAD  A6,DEXWK3 .   SBW    @C@@@@         LOAD  X3,R1 .       GET LOODD
)@@G@@P COUNT     @E@@@@         LOAD  X5,A2 .       SAVE START OF DOPE VECTORDE
)@@G@@ (NEW)@E@@@@         LOAD  A5,W1,X2 .    SAVE ORIGINAL VIRTUAL ORIGIN   DF
)@@G@@@D@@@@         LOAD  A3,W1+1,*X2 . TRANSFER STRING LENGTHS  @C@@@@      DG
)@@G@@   STORE A3,W1+1,*A2 . TO NEW DOPE VECTOR @#@@@@EXCRS3   LABEL .  @H@@@@DH
)@@G@@         JNS   A6,EXCRS4 .   -> RIGHTMOST SBW BIT ON, SUBSCRIPT IS NON-SDI
)@@G@@TAR   @F@@@@ . MULTIPLIER AND BOUNDS OF STARRED SUBSCRIPT BECOME MULTIPLDJ
)@@G@@IER   @B@@@@ . AND BOUNDS OF CROSS SECTION DOPE VECTOR@G@@@@         LOADK
)@@G@@DD A3,W1,*X2 .   COPY MULTIPLIER, EXTENT-1, AND LOWER BOUND @F@@@@      DL
)@@G@@   STORED A3,W1,*A2 .  MOVING POINTER TO NEXT SLOT IN NEW DV@G@@@@      DM
)@@G@@   LOADXM  X1,W1U+1,X1 .     BUMP TO NEXT SLOT IN SUBSCRIPT LIST  @E@@@@DN
)@@G@@EXCRS8   LABEL .                   TRY FOR MORE STORAGE     @D@@@@      DO
)@@G@@   LOAD    A4,W1U,A2 .       SEE IF IT WILL FIT @E@@@@         IF    A4,DP
)@@G@@LT,ADPCND THEN,EXCRS5 . ->WILL IT FIT?    @E@@@@         LINK    WROVFL DQ
)@@G@@.          TRY TO GET MORE STORAGE  @E@@@@         GOTO  EXCRS8 .      -DR
)@@G@@> STILL WITHIN STACK BOUNDS   @#@@@@EXCRS4   LABEL .  @D@@@@         LOADS
)@@G@@D  A4,W1,*X1 .   PICK UP SUBSCRIPT VALUE  @E@@@@         LOAD  A3,W1+1,XDT
)@@G@@2 .  GET EXTENT-1 AND LOWER BOUND   @H@@@@         TLE,XU A4,0,*A3 .TESTDU
)@@G@@ SUBSCRIPT AGAINST LOWER BOUND AND COMPUTE UPPER@D@@@@         GOTO  EXCDV
)@@G@@RCL .      -> SUBSCRIPT TOO LOW     @^@@@@         USING WORD,A3 .@F@@@@DW
)@@G@@         IF    A4,GE,W1XU+1 THEN,EXCRCU . -> SUBSCRIPT TOO HIGH   @E@@@@DX
)@@G@@EXCRSE   LABEL .             MERGE AFTER ERROR CORRECTION   @H@@@@      DY
)@@G@@   MPYS  A4,W1,*X2 .   SUBSCRIPT*MULTIPLIER, ADVANCE OLD DV POINTER     DZ
)@@G@@@E@@@@         ADD   A5,A4 .       ACCUMULATE WITH VIRTUAL ORIGIN @#@@@@EA
)@@G@@EXCRS5   LABEL .  @E@@@@         LOOP  X3,EXCRS3 .   -> REPEAT FOR EACH EB
)@@G@@SUBSCRIPT   @D@@@@         STORE A5,W1,*X5 .   INSERT NEW VIRTUAL ORIGINEC
)@@G@@@F@@@@         IF    A2,NE,X5 THEN,EXCRS6 . -> CROSS SECTION IS AN ARRAYED
)@@G@@@ @@@@         USING SDSECT,A1 .    @E@@@@         IF    SDARST,ON,SDCLSEE
)@@G@@1 THEN,EXCRS6 . -> STRING     @F@@@@         SUB   A2,1,I .      SCALER,EF
)@@G@@ NON-STRING USES ONLY 1 WORD  @I@@@@EXCRS6   LABEL .             CONTINUEG
)@@G@@E SEARCHING THROUNG STRUCTURE FOR BASE ELEME    @H@@@@         IF    A1,EH
)@@G@@EQ,DEXWK1 THEN,EXCRS7 . -> WE'RE BACK TO ORIGINAL SD, DONE  @F@@@@      EI
)@@G@@   IF    SDBROT,NZERO THEN,EXCRS9 . -> FOLLOW SD TO BROTHER @E@@@@      EJ
)@@G@@   LOAD  A1,SDDAD,A1 . -> TEST FATHER FOR BROTHER, ETC@^@@@@         GOTEK
)@@G@@O  EXCRS6 . @#@@@@EXCRS9   LABEL .  @G@@@@         LOAD  A1,SDBROT,A1 . EL
)@@G@@         FOLLOW SD POINTER TO BROTHER     @^@@@@         GOTO  EXCRS1 . EM
)@@G@@@#@@@@EXCRS7   LABEL .  @^@@@@         LOADXI A2,0,I .@F@@@@         TNGEN
)@@G@@,XH2 A2,DEXMAX-(IN 63,H2,1,0) . TEST FOR NEW STACK MAX@D@@@@         STOEO
)@@G@@RE A2,DEXMAX .   SET NEW MAX STACK HEIGHT @E@@@@         STORE A2,AREPTREP
)@@G@@ .   NEW TOP OF ACTIVATION RECORD   @D@@@@         LOAD  A1,DEXWK2+FH2 .EQ
)@@G@@         POINT TO NEW DV@^@@@@         LINK  EXUNSV . @F@@@@         JMPER
)@@G@@   2 .           -> RETURN SKIPPING ARGUMENT LIST     @#@@@@EXCRCL   LABES
)@@G@@EL .  @C@@@@         LOAD  A4,W1XU,X2 .  USE LOWER BOUND    @#@@@@EXCRCEET
)@@G@@   LABEL .  @D@@@@         LOAD    X4,X1 .           HOLD FOR LATER     EU
)@@G@@@E@@@@         LOAD    X1,R1 .           GET NUMBER OF DIMS-1     @E@@@@EV
)@@G@@         SUB     X1,W1U,X3 .       SUB OFF NUMBER LEFT-1    @D@@@@      EW
)@@G@@   ADD     X1,1,I .          MAKE ONE ORIGIN    @E@@@@         ONUNIT  EEX
)@@G@@REXSB,ACCDSU,2  R,I,R  DEXWK1,4  DEXMAX,4 @D@@@@         LOAD    X1,X4 .EY
)@@G@@           RECLAIM REGISTER   @E@@@@ . 'SUBSCRIPT ', X1, ' OF ', SDA1, 'EZ
)@@G@@ IS OUT OF BOUNDS.'     @C@@@@         GOTO  EXCRSE .      -> RETURN TO FA
)@@G@@CALLER@#@@@@EXCRCU   LABEL .  @C@@@@         LOAD  A4,W1XU,A3 .  USE UPPFB
)@@G@@ER BOUND    @^@@@@         GOTO  EXCRCE . @E@@@@         END . EXECUTIONFC

)@@G@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@*[@@@@*SDFF*@ @@@@      SUBROUTINE S1INEP(K)    EJ
)@@G@@@ @@@@      IMPLICIT INTEGER (A-Z)  @[@@@@C     @[@@@@C     @F@@@@C     EK

)@@G@@NT .EQ. LCOUNT) RETURN  @#@@@@      LCOUNT=COUNT@#@@@@      IRERR=.TRUE.EQ

)@@G@@     -HICH WAS READ AS FOLLOWS  )   @]@@@@      RETURN@[@@@@C     @ @@@@EU

)@@G@@S)    @B@@[]251   CALL S1INPI( C(LCARDS), NCR, CHARS) @][@@@      RETURNEW

)@@G@@S9INIT*.            SUBROUTINE S9INIT(CARD,OFFSET)    @F@@@@          LAFX
)@@G@@,U      A0,*0,X11.        CARD IMAGE BASE ADDRESS     @D@@@@          LAFY
)@@G@@,U      A1,*1,X11.        OFFSET ADDRESS  @ @@@@          SA,H2     A1,OFZ
)@@G@@FFSET @A@@@@          AA        A0,(0400000)    @ @@@@          SA,H2   GA
)@@G@@  A0,CH1    @ @@@@          SA,H2     A0,CH2    @ @@@@          J       GB
)@@G@@  3,X11.    @D@@@@S9FRST*.            ENTRY S9FRST(EXTRACHARACTERS)     GC
)@@G@@@F@@@@OFFSET    LA        A3,$.             GET OFFSET FOR INITIAL SHIFTGD
)@@G@@@ @@@@          LA        A0,(1,1). @E@@@@          LA,U      A2,10.    GE
)@@G@@       CUT-OFF FOR STAR SCAN  @F@@@@CH1       L         A5,$,*A0.       GF
)@@G@@  PICK UP WORD FROM CARD IMAGE@F@@@@          LSSL      A5,0,A3.        GG
)@@G@@  GET RID OF 'ELL' OR 'ROUP'  @^@@@@          SZ        A4. @E@@@@      GH
)@@G@@    LDSL      A4,6.             GET NEXT CHARACTER    @F@@@@          TEGI
)@@G@@,U      A4,STAR.          STAR IS FIELDATA CODE FOR * @ @@@@          J GJ
)@@G@@        START-1   @E@@@@          JNZ       A5,$-4.           J TO SZ A4GK
)@@G@@. IF A *    @D@@@@.                   UNLESS NEED A NEW WORD OF DATA    GL
)@@G@@@G@@@@          EX        CH1.             GET ANOTHER WORD, INCREMENT AGM
)@@G@@0     @G@@@@          JGD       A2,CH1+2.        J TO   SZ A4   UNLESS TGN
)@@G@@OO MANY *'S @G@@@@          SA        A2,*0,X11.       SET EXTRA CHARACTGO
)@@G@@ER COUNT TO -1    @C@@@@          J         2,X11.           RETURN     GP
)@@G@@@G@@@@          DSL       A4,6.             IF A LEGAL ID CHARACTER WAS GQ
)@@G@@SHIFT-@F@@@@.                   ED INTO A4, SHIFT IT BACK BEFORE STARTINGR
)@@G@@G     @F@@@@START     SZ        A1.               A1 COUNTS EXTRA CHARACGS
)@@G@@TERS  @B@@@@          DL        A2,('@@@@@A      ')   @^@@@@          SZGT
)@@G@@        A4. @G@@@@          JNZ       A5,CH2+1.         KEEP PROCESSING GU
)@@G@@IF DON'T NEED MORE@E@@@@          TNE       A0,LIMIT.         CHECK FOR GV
)@@G@@END OF CARD @ @@@@          J         DONE.     @D@@@@CH2       LA      GW
)@@G@@  A5,$,*A0.         GET ANOTHER WORD@D@@@@          LDSL      A4,6.     GX
)@@G@@        PUT CHAR IN A4  @E@@@@          TNE,XU    A4,COMMA.         COMMGY
)@@G@@A IS FIELDATA ,   @F@@@@          J         DONE.             IF A COMMAGZ
)@@G@@, HAVE WORD IN A3 @D@@@@          TNE,XU    A4,5.             IS IT A BLHA
)@@G@@ANK   @D@@@@          J         START+2.          IF SO, JUMP     @ @@@@HB
)@@G@@          JZ        A2,TOOBIG.@D@@@@          LSSL      A4,30.          HC
)@@G@@  PUT CHAR ON LEFT@D@@@@          LDSL      A3,6.             SHIFT IT IHD
)@@G@@NTO A3@D@@@@          JGD       A2,START+3.       ALWAYS JUMPS    @ @@@@HE
)@@G@@DONE      MSI,XU    A2,6.     @E@@@@          LSSC      A3,0,A2.        HF
)@@G@@  LEFT ADJUST THE ID    @D@@@@          SA        A0,SAVE.          SAVEHG
)@@G@@ FOR NEXT ID@ @@@@          S         A5,SAVE+1.@E@@@@          LA      HH
)@@G@@  A0,A3.            RETURN VALUE IN A0    @ @@@@          J         2,X1HI
)@@G@@1.    @F@@@@          SA        A1,*0,X11.        SAVE # OF EXTRA CHARACHJ
)@@G@@TERS  @F@@@@TOOBIG    AA,XU     A1,1.             COUNT OF EXTRA CHARACTHK
)@@G@@ERS   @ @@@@          J         START+3   @G@@@@S9NEXT*.            ENTRHL
)@@G@@Y S9NEXT(EXTRACHARACTERS)   FOR ALL IDS AFTER   @B@@@@.                 HM
)@@G@@  THE FIRST FROM A CARD @ @@@@          LA        A0,SAVE.  @ @@@@      HN
)@@G@@    LA        A5,SAVE+1.@ @@@@          J         START.    @#@@@@      HO
)@@G@@    END     ___IAL SHIFT)@]@C@)@@[]^[#@[@K[@@@@@C@0@@B/KF@@#[^@@@W[^@@@EHP
)@@G@@G@@@@#[^K@@BC8VK@[C8FK@@@@[@@IAA@@@@)@C[N#@@K@[@K^@@@@')@@@E/ K@@G/K@@@PHQ
)@@G@@%9@@@*;!@@@A @@@@K;(Z@@@C[W)@EC8)@@EC@@@@^AB@@@@)@M[N@@^G@[@K0@K@@/K@@@&HR
)@@G@@:@@@@]/ K@@X @@@@K9?)@@  @@@@H;H@@@A/KF@@][@:K@@8#)@@GAC@@@@)@W[N@[@^[@[HS

)@@G@@SUBROUTINE S1FMTI(MAXSET,MINSET,M)  @A@@@@      DATA MAXSIG/8/, MINSIG/4HZ
)@@G@@/     @#@@@@      INTEGER TYPE@^@@@@      DIMENSION X(2)    @^@@@@      IA
)@@G@@DEFINE ADD=1.E-7  @#@@@@      LOGICAL IS  @^@@@@      DATA IS/.FALSE./  IB
)@@G@@@[@@@@C     @ @@@@      DATA  IWORD/'XXX.XX'/   @F@@@@C         THE  4 TIC
)@@G@@H CHARACTER POSITION (FROM THE LEFT) OF IWORD IS@G@@@@C         ALWAYS LID
)@@G@@EFT AS THE DECIMAL POINT SET IN THE ABOVE STATEMENT   @#@@@@      DEFINEIE
)@@G@@ F=11 @D@@@@C         11 (DECIMAL) IS THE INTERNAL BCD CODE FOR  F@#@@@@IF
)@@G@@      DEFINE G=12 @D@@@@C         12 (DECIMAL) IS THE INTERNAL BCD CODE IG
)@@G@@FOR  G@A@@@@      DEFINE TYPE=FLD(0,6,IWORD)    @[@@@@C     @^@@@@      IH
)@@G@@MAXSIG=MAXSET     @^@@@@      MINSIG=MINSET     @]@@@@      MODE=M@]@@@@II
)@@G@@      RETURN@G@@@@C         END OF INITIALIZATION TO OVERRIDE PRE-SET MAIJ
)@@G@@XSIG AND MINSIG   @[@@@@C     @D@@@@      ENTRY S1FMT3(X,LL,IWIDE,IAFTERIK
)@@G@@,JWORD,NEXTRA)    @]@@@@      L=LL  @#@@@@      IFNEG=-1    @^@@@@      IL
)@@G@@IEXTRA=NEXTRA     @#@@@@      XX=X(1)     @ @@@@      IF(L.EQ.1)GO TO 30IM
)@@G@@0     @#@@@@      XMAX=ABS(XX)@#@@@@      XMIN=XMAX   @#@@@@      DO 20 IN
)@@G@@I=2,L @#@@@@      XX=X(I)     @A@@@@      IF(ABS(XX).LE.XMAX)GO TO 10   IO
)@@G@@@#@@@@      XMAX=ABS(XX)@#@@@@      GO TO 20    @B@@@@10    IF(ABS(XX).LIP
)@@G@@T.XMIN)XMIN=ABS(XX)     @^@@@@20    IF(XX.LT.0)IFNEG=0@F@@@@C         NOIQ
)@@G@@W IFNEG=0 IF ANY X(I) ARE NEGATIVE,  =-1 OTHERWISE    @[@@@@C     @A@@@@IR
)@@G@@      IF(XMAX.EQ.XMIN)GO TO 310     @#@@@@100   AL=-50.     @]@@@@      IS
)@@G@@NMIN=1@]@@@@      NMAX=1@^@@@@      AH=LOG10(XMAX)    @A@@@@      IF(XMIIT
)@@G@@N.NE.0)AL=LOG10(XMIN)   @^@@@@      IF(AL)   ,110,120 @#@@@@      NMIN=AIU
)@@G@@L+ADD @^@@@@110   IF(AH)   ,140,130 @#@@@@      NMAX=AH+ADD @#@@@@      IV
)@@G@@GO TO 140   @^@@@@120   NMIN=INT(AL)+1    @^@@@@130   NMAX=INT(AH)+1    IW
)@@G@@@#@@@@140   IT=NMAX     @A@@@@      IF(IT.GT.MAXSIG)GO TO 410     @B@@@@IX
)@@G@@      IF(IT.LT.MINSIG-MAXSIG)GO TO 410    @^@@@@      FLD(0,6,IWORD)=F  IY
)@@G@@@^@@@@      IF(IT.LT.0)NMAX=0 @^@@@@      NAFTER=MINSIG-NMIN@ @@@@      IZ
)@@G@@IF(NAFTER.LT.0)NAFTER=0 @A@@@@      NWIDE=NMAX+NAFTER+IFNEG+3     @^@@@@JA
)@@G@@      IF(IS)GO TO 620   @B@@@@      IF(MAXSIG.GE.NMAX+NAFTER)GO TO 210  JB
)@@G@@@ @@@@      IF(MODE.NE.0)GO TO 410  @F@@@@C         MODE=0 IS MEANS MODEJC
)@@G@@, AND IS WILLING TO GIVE FEW OR NO  @G@@@@C         SIGNIFICANT DIGITS FJD
)@@G@@OR VERY SMALL NUMBERS (COMPARED TO THE    @C@@@@C         LARGEST IN THEJE
)@@G@@ SET TO BE PRINTED)     @G@@@@C         MODE=1  IMPLIES ALL NON-ZERO NUMJF
)@@G@@BERS MUST HAVE SIG DIGITS     @E@@@@C170      LEADING DIGITS OF XMAX ANDJG
)@@G@@ XMIN ARE TOO FAR APART.@D@@@@C         THIS IS DUE TO DIFFERENCES IN MAJH
)@@G@@GNITUDE.    @F@@@@C         USE MAXSIG SIGNIFICANT DIGITS FOR XMAX, AND JI
)@@G@@DON'T WORRY @D@@@@C         ABOUT THE NUMBERS OF SMALLER MAGNITUDE.     JJ
)@@G@@@^@@@@170   NAFTER=MAXSIG-IT  @A@@@@      NWIDE=NMAX+NAFTER+IFNEG+3     JK
)@@G@@@F@@@@C210      COMPOSE WORD, THE WORD CONTAINING THE FORMAT ITSELF.    JL
)@@G@@@E@@@@C         NOTE THAT NWIDE AND NAFTER ARE ALSO RETURNED.     @F@@@@JM
)@@G@@C         NOTE THAT THIS FORMAT DOES NOT INCLUDE THE PARENTHESES. @#@@@@JN
)@@G@@210   CONTINUE    @[@@@@C     @^@@@@      I10=NAFTER/10     @^@@@@      JO
)@@G@@I01=NAFTER-10*I10 @ @@@@      FLD(30,6,IWORD)=I01+48  @ @@@@      FLD(24JP
)@@G@@,6,IWORD)=I10+48  @E@@@@C         IEXTRA IS NEXTRA FOR S1FMT1,2,3  AND 0JQ
)@@G@@ FOR S1FMTW @^@@@@      NWIDE=NWIDE+IEXTRA@#@@@@      I10=NWIDE/10@^@@@@JR
)@@G@@      I01=NWIDE-10*I10  @ @@@@      FLD(12,6,IWORD)=I01+48  @ @@@@      JS
)@@G@@FLD(6,6,IWORD)=I10+48   @#@@@@      JWORD=IWORD @ @@@@      IF(.NOT.IS)GJT
)@@G@@O TO 220    @#@@@@      IS=.FALSE.  @]@@@@      RETURN@#@@@@220   IWIDE=JU
)@@G@@NWIDE @^@@@@      IAFTER=NAFTER     @]@@@@      RETURN@[@@@@C     @G@@@@JV
)@@G@@C         ENTRY WHEN FORMAT IS DESIRED FOR PRINTING ONLY 1 NUMBER, W    JW
)@@G@@@[@@@@C     @C@@@@      ENTRY S1FMT1(W,IWIDE,IAFTER,JWORD,NEXTRA) @[@@@@JX
)@@G@@C     @^@@@@      IEXTRA=NEXTRA     @#@@@@      IFNEG=-1    @]@@@@      JY
)@@G@@XX=W  @[@@@@C     @B@@@@C300      ONLY ONE NUMBER IS TO BE PRINTED@^@@@@JZ
)@@G@@300   IF(XX.LT.0)IFNEG=0@#@@@@      XMAX=ABS(XX)@F@@@@C310      XMAX=XMIKA
)@@G@@N AS DETERMINED ABOVE CAUSES A JUMP TO HERE     @ @@@@310   IF(XMAX.EQ.0KB
)@@G@@)GO TO 380  @^@@@@      AH=LOG10(XMAX)    @]@@@@      NMAX=1@^@@@@      KC
)@@G@@IF(AH)   ,340,320 @#@@@@      NMAX=AH+ADD @#@@@@      GO TO 330   @^@@@@KD
)@@G@@320   NMAX=INT(AH)+1    @A@@@@330   IF(NMAX.GT.MAXSIG)GO TO 410   @B@@@@KE
)@@G@@      IF(NMAX.LT.MINSIG-MAXSIG)GO TO 410  @]@@@@340   TYPE=F@^@@@@      KF
)@@G@@NAFTER=MINSIG-NMAX@ @@@@      IF(NAFTER.LT.0)NAFTER=0 @A@@@@      NWIDE=KG
)@@G@@NMAX+NAFTER+IFNEG+3     @^@@@@      IF(IS)GO TO 610   @#@@@@      GO TO KH
)@@G@@210   @[@@@@C     @C@@@@C380      ONLY HAVE TO PRINT THE NUMBER ZERO    KI
)@@G@@@[@@@@C     @#@@@@380   NAFTER=0    @#@@@@      NWIDE=6     @]@@@@      KJ
)@@G@@TYPE=F@^@@@@      IF(IS)NWIDE=INWIDE@C@@@@C         NO NEED TO GO TO THEKK
)@@G@@ 600 STATEMENTS   @#@@@@      GO TO 210   @F@@@@C410      NEED A G OR E KL
)@@G@@FIELD TO HANDLE NUMBERS OF THIS MAGNITUDE.@#@@@@410   CONTINUE    @^@@@@KM
)@@G@@      IF(IS)GO TO 420   @]@@@@      TYPE=G@^@@@@      NAFTER=MINSIG     KN
)@@G@@@ @@@@      NWIDE=NAFTER+IFNEG+6    @#@@@@      GO TO 210   @#@@@@420   KO
)@@G@@NWIDE=INWIDE@#@@@@      GO TO 640   @[@@@@C     @[@@@@C     @G@@@@C     KP
)@@G@@    ENTRY WHEN MAXIMUM AND MINIMUM MAGNITUDES OF NUMBERS TO BE    @A@@@@KQ
)@@G@@C         PRINTED ARE ALREADY KNOWN @[@@@@C     @[@@@@C     @D@@@@      KR
)@@G@@ENTRY S1FMT2(Y,Z,IWIDE,IAFTER,JWORD,NEXTRA)     @F@@@@C         THE CALLKS
)@@G@@ING PROGRAM CAN MAKE EITHER OF THE FIRST TWO    @G@@@@C         PARAMETEKT
)@@G@@RS NEGATIVE TO FORCE ALLOWING FOR THE PRINTING OF     @ @@@@C         NEKU
)@@G@@GATIVE NUMBERS    @G@@@@C         HOWEVER, REMEMBER THAT THESE PARAMETERKV
)@@G@@S ARE THE MAX AND MIN   @G@@@@C         MAGNITUDES, AND NOT THE MAXIMUM KW
)@@G@@AND MINIMUM VALUES OF THE     @A@@@@C         NUMBERS TO BE PRINTED.    KX
)@@G@@@[@@@@C     @^@@@@      IEXTRA=NEXTRA     @#@@@@500   CONTINUE    @#@@@@KY
)@@G@@      IFNEG=-1    @^@@@@      IF(Y.LT.0)IFNEG=0 @^@@@@      IF(Z.LT.0)IFKZ
)@@G@@NEG=0 @E@@@@C         THE MAX MAG AND MINMAG CAN BE IN EITHER ORDER     LA
)@@G@@@D@@@@C         THE SUBROUTINE WILL STRAIGHTEN THEM OUT     @G@@@@C     LB
)@@G@@    THIS IS EASIER THAN DETECTING THE ERROR AND NOT CORRECTING    @F@@@@LC
)@@G@@C         IT, PRINTING AN ERROR MESSAGE AND RETURNING GARBAGE.    @[@@@@LD
)@@G@@C     @A@@@@      IF(ABS(Y).GT.ABS(Z))GO TO 510 @#@@@@      XMAX=ABS(Z) LE
)@@G@@@#@@@@      XMIN=ABS(Y) @#@@@@      GO TO 520   @#@@@@510   XMAX=ABS(Y) LF

)@@G@@=0    @#@@@@      IS=.TRUE.   @#@@@@      GO TO 500   @B@@@@C610      F LI
)@@G@@FORMAT, 1 # TO BE PRINTED     @#@@@@610   CONTINUE    @#@@@@      NMIN=NLJ

)@@G@@ MORE #'S TO BE PRINTED @D@@@@C         ARRIVE WITH NMAX,NMIN,NAFTER,NWILL
)@@G@@DE  DEFINED @#@@@@620   CONTINUE    @^@@@@      IT=NWIDE-INWIDE   @#@@@@LM
)@@G@@      NWIDE=INWIDE@^@@@@      IF(IT)210,210     @^@@@@C630      NWIDE > LN
)@@G@@INWIDE@B@@@@C         THUS A NARROWER FIELD IS NEEDED @B@@@@C         IFLO
)@@G@@ XMIN _ 0, NEED MINSIG PLACES @F@@@@C         IF XMIN = 0,  DON'T WORRY LP
)@@G@@ABOUT THE NUMBER OF PLACES    @C@@@@C         PRINTED FOR XMIN. [ONLY XMLQ
)@@G@@AX MATTERS] @ @@@@630   IF(XMIN.NE.0)GO TO 640  @^@@@@      NAFTER=NAFTELR
)@@G@@R-IT  @ @@@@      IF(NAFTER)   ,210,210   @#@@@@      NAFTER=0    @B@@@@LS
)@@G@@      IF(NWIDE.GE.NMAX+IFNEG+3)GOTO 210   @D@@@@C         GO TO 210 IF TLT
)@@G@@HIS FIELD WIDTH WILL WORK     @B@@@@C         OTHERWISE, FALL THROUGH TOLU
)@@G@@ 640  @[@@@@C     @G@@@@C         JUMP TO 640 FROM 630 IF WANT MINSIG DILV
)@@G@@GITS FOR XMIN IF AT ALL @E@@@@C         POSSIBLE, INSTEAD OF TRYING FIRSLW
)@@G@@T FOR F FORMAT.   @#@@@@640   CONTINUE    @^@@@@      FLD(0,6,IWORD)=G  LX
)@@G@@@B@@@@      NAFTER=MIN(NWIDE-6-IFNEG,MINSIG)    @ @@@@      IF(NAFTER)  LY
)@@G@@ ,   ,210   @F@@@@C         IF G FORMAT WON'T WORK, GIVE UP AND RETURN ALZ
)@@G@@N INADEQUATE@ @@@@C         FORMAT IN JWORD.    @^@@@@      FLD(0,6,IWORMA
)@@G@@D)=F  @#@@@@      NAFTER=0    @#@@@@      GO TO 210   @[@@@@C     @]@@@@MB
)@@G@@      END   ___   @A@@@@C         PRINTED ARE ALREADY KNOWN @[@@@@C     MC

)@@G@@@B@@@@S9ZERO*.            SUBROUTINE S9ZERO(X,N)@D@@@@          LA,U    OQ

)@@G@@        INCREMENT @C@@@@          LR        R1,*1,X11.        # OF WORDSOS

)@@G@@          JGD       R1,$-1.   @C@@@@          J         3,X11.          OU
)@@G@@  RETURN    @D@@@@S9SIZE*.            INTEGER FUNCTION S9SIZE(KT,N)     OV
)@@G@@@ @@@@          LA,U      A1,*0,X11.@ @@@@          LXI,XU    A1,1.     OW
)@@G@@@C@@@@          LA        A0,0,A1.          KT(1)     @C@@@@          LROX
)@@G@@        R1,*1,X11.        COUNT     @F@@@@          SNE       A0,0,*A1. OY
)@@G@@        SKIP WHEN NOT EQUAL FOUND   @G@@@@          J         3,X11.    OZ
)@@G@@        ALL CELL SIZES=FIRST, RETURN IN A0@G@@@@          SZ        A0. PA
)@@G@@              UNEQUAL SIZES, RETURN 0 IN A0     @ @@@@          J       PB
)@@G@@  3,X11.    @C@@@@S9MT*.              INTEGER FUNCTION S9MT(KT,N) @G@@@@PC
)@@G@@.         SEARCHES FOR EMPTY CELLS. RETURNS THE NUMBER OF EMPTY CELLS   PD
)@@G@@@#@@@@.         IN AO   @[@@@@.     @G@@@@          SZ        A0.       PE
)@@G@@        RETURNED COUNT OF EMPTY CELLS     @E@@@@          SZ        A1. PF
)@@G@@              ZERO USED FOR SEARCH  @G@@@@          LA,U      A2,*0,X11.PG
)@@G@@        KT BASE ADDRESS USED FOR STORE    @C@@@@          LXI,XU    A2,1PH
)@@G@@.             INCREMENT @G@@@@          LA        A3,A2.            KT BPI
)@@G@@ASE ADDRESS USED FOR SEARCH   @D@@@@          LR        R1,*1,X11.      PJ
)@@G@@  COUNT FOR SEARCH@F@@@@SE        SE        A1,0,*A3.         SKIP IF COPK
)@@G@@UNT OF ZERO FOUND @ @@@@          J         3,X11.    @E@@@@          AAPL
)@@G@@,XU     A0,1.             BUMP # OF EMPTY CELLS @^@@@@          J       PM
)@@G@@  SE  @#@@@@          END     ___@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@PN

)@@G@@*[@@@@*SDFF*@A@@@@      SUBROUTINE S15INI(C,NS,$,INP) @ @@@@      DIMENSQR
)@@G@@ION C(2),INP(2)   @ @@@@      IMPLICIT INTEGER(A-Z)   @#@@@@      COMMONQS
)@@G@@ X(2) @^@@@@      DEFINE XX(I)=X(I) @C@@@@      CALL S1GTAG('LCARDS',INDQT
)@@G@@,NWE,NEL,$997)    @#@@@@      CHARS=80    @B@@@@      CALL S1GVAL('CHARSQU
)@@G@@',CHARS,$15,$15)  @^@@@@   15 WORDS= (CHARS+5)/6@^@@@@      CHARS=WORDS*QV
)@@G@@6     @[@@@@C     @G@@@@C        NEW MATRIX WILL CONTAIN INFORMATION WHEQW
)@@G@@RE TO FIND INPUT RECORD @[@@@@C     @#@@@@      DO 40 I=1,NS@A@@@@      QX
)@@G@@C(I)=(C(I+NS)-1)*CHARS + C(I) @A@@@@      C(I+NS)=(C(I)-(C(I)/6)*6-1)*6 QY
)@@G@@@^@@@@      C(I)=(C(I)+5)/6   @A@@@@      IF(C(I+NS).GE.0) GO TO 20     QZ
)@@G@@@#@@@@      C(I+NS)=30  @ @@@@   20 C(I)=C(I)+IND+WORDS-1   @ @@@@      RA
)@@G@@C(I+NS)=ABS(C(I+NS))    @#@@@@   40 CONTINUE    @]@@@@      RETURN@[@@@@RB
)@@G@@C     @ @@@@C        GET NEW INPUT RECORD @[@@@@C     @A@@@@      ENTRY RC
)@@G@@S15INP(INP,IFLAG,$)     @ @@@@      CALL S1INOB(DUM,FLAG)   @ @@@@      RD
)@@G@@IF (FLAG+1) 50,999,70   @#@@@@   50 IFLAG=1     @]@@@@      RETURN@#@@@@RE
)@@G@@   70 DO 80 I=1,NS@#@@@@      IDUM=C(I+NS)@A@@@@      INP(I)=FLD(IDUM,6,RF
)@@G@@XX(C(I)))   @#@@@@   80 CONTINUE    @^@@@@      IF(FLAG-1)  ,85,85@]@@@@RG
)@@G@@      RETURN@#@@@@   85 IFLAG=2     @]@@@@      RETURN@#@@@@  997 PRINT RH
)@@G@@998   @F@@@@  998 FORMAT(1H0,'ANALYSIS ABANDONED.TAG  LCARDS WAS NOT FOURI
)@@G@@ND.') @#@@@@  999 RETURN 3    @]@@@@      END   ___@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@RJ
)@@G@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@RK
)@@G@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@RL

)@@G@@*[@@@@*SDFF*@A@@@@      SUBROUTINE S15RDC(C1,C,NS)    @#@@@@      INTEGESO
)@@G@@R C1,C@A@@[@      DIMENSION C(NS,2),C1(2,100)   @#[@@@      IREAD=0     SP
)@@G@@@B@@[@      CALL S1IODR(5,'REWIND',LEND,C1,LEND)@#[@@@      ISTOR=0     SQ
)@@G@@@B@@[@    5 CALL S1IODR(5,'READ',200,C1,LEND)   @^[@@@      IREAD=IREAD+SR
)@@G@@1     @^@@@@      DO 10 I=1,100     @A@@[@      IF(C1(1,I).EQ.(-1)) GO TSS
)@@G@@O 30  @#[@@@      IDUM=ISTOR+I@ @@@@      IF(IDUM.GT.NS) GO TO 15 @^@@[@ST
)@@G@@      C(IDUM,1)=C1(1,I) @^@@[@      C(IDUM,2)=C1(2,I) @#]@@@   10 CONTINSU
)@@G@@UE    @^@@@@      ISTOR=ISTOR+100   @#@@@@      GO TO 5     @#@@@@   15 SV
)@@G@@PRINT 20    @D@@@@   20 FORMAT('0ERROR IN S15RDC.REPORT TO CONSULTANT.')SW
)@@G@@@]@@@@   30 RETURN@]@@@@      END   ___@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@SX

)@@G@@*[@@@@*SDFF*@B@@@@      SUBROUTINE S15PRC(OUT,K,ISW,IPSW)   @G@@@@C-OUT UL
)@@G@@- ARRAY TO BE PRINTED OUT, K IS THE NUMBER OF ITS ELEMENTS(USUALLY@^@@@@UM
)@@G@@C-        IT IS 20)     @G@@@@C-ISW=1 PRINTS THE FIRST ROW OF THE HEADINUN
)@@G@@G FOR A LIST,  ISW=2 PRINTS   @G@@@@C-    THE SECOND ROW OF THE HEADING UO
)@@G@@FOR A LIST,  ISW=3 PRINTS THE FIRST @B@@@@C-     ROW OF THE HEADING ON AUP
)@@G@@ NEW PAGE   @ @@@@      IMPLICIT INTEGER (A-Z)  @#@@@@      REAL OUTR   UQ
)@@G@@@^@@@@      DIMENSION OUTR(2) @ @@@@      DIMENSION OUT(2),C(20)  @#@@@@UR
)@@G@@      DO 40 I=1,K @#@@@@      NN=OUT(I)   @A@@@@      CALL S1ENCI(NN,C(IUS
)@@G@@),5,5,1)    @]@@@@      II=12 @ @@@@      IF(NN.LT.100) GO TO 30  @^@@@@UT
)@@G@@      IF(NN.LE.9999)II=0@^@@@@      IF(NN.LE.999)II=6 @^@@@@   30 IF(NN.UU
)@@G@@LE.9)II=18  @ @@@@      IF(ISW.NE.2) GO TO 35   @^@@@@      FLD(II,6,C(IUV
)@@G@@))=41 @^@@@@      FLD(30,6,C(I))=32 @#@@@@      GO TO 40    @^@@@@   35 UW
)@@G@@FLD(II,6,C(I))=40 @^@@@@      FLD(30,6,C(I))=40 @#@@@@   40 CONTINUE    UX
)@@G@@@ @@@@      GO TO (50,60,45),ISW    @#@@@@   45 CALL S1PHED @#@@@@      UY
)@@G@@ITSW=IPSW+1 @ @@@@      GO TO (46,48) ,ITSW     @#@@@@   46 PRINT 100   UZ
)@@G@@@D@@[@  100 FORMAT(28X,'F R E Q U E N C Y    C O U N T S')  @#[@@@      VA
)@@G@@GO TO 49    @#@@@@   48 PRINT 110   @B@@[@  110 FORMAT(28X,'P E R C E N VB
)@@G@@T A G E S') @#[@@@   49 PRINT 47    @G@@@@   47 FORMAT(1H0,27X,'COLUMN NVC
)@@G@@UMBERS ENCLOSED WITHIN  * *    CARD WITHIN@B@@@@     * INPUT RECORD ENCLVD
)@@G@@OSED WITHIN  ( )')@ @@@@   50 PRINT 55,(C(I),I=1,K)   @A@@[@   55 FORMATVE
)@@G@@(1H0,'PUNCH',6X,20A6)   @][@@@      RETURN@ @@@@   60 PRINT 70,(C(I),I=1VF
)@@G@@,K)   @A@@@@   70 FORMAT(1H ,'CODE  CHAR ',20A6)@#@@@@      PRINT 75    VG
)@@G@@@#@@@@   75 FORMAT(1H ) @]@@@@      RETURN@A@@@@C-PRINT ONE ROW OF FREQUVH
)@@G@@ENCY COUNTS @B@@@@      ENTRY S15PRT(OUT,K,CHAR1,CHAR2)     @B@@@@      VI
)@@G@@PRINT 80,CHAR1,CHAR2,(OUT(I),I=1,K) @A@@@@   80 FORMAT(1X,A6,2X,R1,1X,20VJ
)@@G@@I6)   @]@@@@      RETURN@B@@@@      ENTRY S15PRP(OUTR,K,CHAR1,CHAR2)    VK
)@@G@@@B@@@@      PRINT 90,CHAR1,CHAR2,(OUTR(I),I=1,K)@A@@@@   90 FORMAT(1X,A6VL
)@@G@@,2X,R1,2X,20F6.1) @]@@@@      RETURN@]@@@@      END   ___@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@VM

)@@G@@*[@@@@*SDFF*@C@@[@      SUBROUTINE S1INV (A,D,DET,IERR,TOL,NV,NR) @D[@@@XD
)@@G@@C         POSITIVE DEFINITE MATRIX INVERSION ROUTINE  @A@@@@C           XE
)@@G@@        NO PIVOTTING    @ @@[@      DIMENSION A(NR,NV),D(NV)@A[@@@C     XF
)@@G@@    A IS MATRIX TO BE INVERTED@A@@@@C                   OF ORDER N=NV   XG
)@@G@@@E@@@@C                   WITH NR ROWS ALLOCATED TO IT IN STORAGE @F@@@@XH
)@@G@@C         D IS SCRATCH BUT HAS SPECIAL USE WITH TOL (SEE BELOW)   @G@@@@XI
)@@G@@C                   CONTAINS DIAGONALS OF INVERSE AFTER FORWARD SECTION XJ
)@@G@@@A@@@@C         DET CONTAINS DETERMINANT  @G@@@@C         IERR IS ERROR XK
)@@G@@FLAG SET TO INDEX OF THE FIRST NEG DIAG ELEMENT @G^@@@C         TOL MUSTXL
)@@G@@ BE GREATER THAN RATIO OF INITIAL DIAGONALS (OR D IF  @G@@@@C           XM
)@@G@@        ITS FIRST WORD IS NON-ZERO) TO SUBSEQUENT DIAGONALS @[@@@@C     XN
)@@G@@@G@@@@C  RESET OVERFLOW INDICATOR---------------------------------------XO
)@@G@@------@#@@@@      CALL S1VFWC @]@@@@      IERR=0@]@@@@      N=NV  @]@@@@XP
)@@G@@      NN=N-1@A[@@@      IF (D(1) .NE. 0) GO TO 100    @#@@@@      DO 75 XQ
)@@G@@J=2,N @#@@@@75    D(J)=A(J,J) @ @@@@C         FORWARD SECTION     @#@@@@XR
)@@G@@100   DET=A(1,1)  @#@@@@      D(1)=DET    @^@@@@      DO 190 I=1,NN     XS
)@@G@@@]@@@@      II=I+1@^@@@@      DO 180 K=II,N     @^@@@@      TEMP=A(I,K)/XT
)@@G@@A(I,I)@^@@@@      DO 170 J=1,NR     @A@@@@170   A(J,K)=A(J,K)-TEMP*A(J,IXU
)@@G@@)     @#@@@@180   A(I,K)=-TEMP@^@@@@      TEMP=A(II,II)     @#@@@@      XV
)@@G@@DET=DET*TEMP@E@@@@      IF (D(II)/TEMP .LT. TOL .AND. TEMP. GT .0) GO TOXW
)@@G@@ 190  @E@@@@C         ERROR RETURN WHEN EXCESSIVE CANCELLATION OCCURS   XX
)@@G@@@#@@@@      IERR=II     @#@@@@      GO TO 900   @^@@@@190   D(II)=SQRT (XY
)@@G@@TEMP) @C@@@@C         FORM DIAGONALS OF INVERSE SECTION     @^@@@@      XZ
)@@G@@DO 250 J=1,NN     @]@@@@      JJ=J+1@^@@@@      TEMP=1.0/A(J,J)   @^@@@@YA
)@@G@@      DO 245 K=JJ,N     @^@@@@      SEMP=A(J,K)/D(K)  @ @@@@      TEMP=TYB
)@@G@@EMP+SEMP*SEMP     @#@@@@245   A(J,K)=SEMP @#@@@@250   D(J)=TEMP   @^@@@@YC
)@@G@@      D(N)=1.0/A(N,N)   @B@@@@C         RETURN IF ONLY FORWARD DESIRED  YD
)@@G@@@ [@@@C         BACKWARD SECTION    @#@@@@300   CONTINUE    @G@@@@C  TESYE
)@@G@@T OVERFLOW INDICATOR++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++@A@@@@YF
)@@G@@900   CALL S1VFWT(6HINV  1,$910)    @]@@@@910   RETURN@]@@@@      END   YG

)@@G@@SUBROUTINE S1TIMI @^@@@@      DIMENSION M(5)    @^@@[@      DATA ISEC/4HAO
)@@G@@SEC./ @#@@[@      DATA T1/0/  @#@@@@      ITEST=0     @B@@@@      CALL SAP
)@@G@@1GVAL('TEST',ITEST,$3,$3)     @#@@@@    3 CONTINUE    @#@@@@      PRINT AQ
)@@G@@1     @D@@@@    1 FORMAT ('0***** ELAPSED TIME RESET TO ZERO')    @^@@[@AR
)@@G@@      T1=URTIMF(DUMMY)  @][@@@      RETURN@^@@@@      ENTRY S1TIMA(I,M) AS
)@@G@@@ @@@@    5 IF (I.LT.1)  GO TO 100  @ @@@@      IF (I.GT.10) GO TO 100  AT
)@@G@@@^@@[@      T2=URTIMF(DUMMY)  @#@@[@      T=T2-T1     @]@@[@      KT=T  AU
)@@G@@@#@@[@      KS=KT/1000  @#@@[@      KV=KS*1000  @#@@[@      KV=KT-KV    AV
)@@G@@@]@@[@      IY=6H.@ @@[@      CALL S1ENCI(KS,IX,6,6,1)@ @@[@      CALL SAW
)@@G@@1ENCI(KV,IY,4,3,0)@B@@[@      PRINT 10,(M(J),J=1,I),IX,IY,ISEC    @]]@@@AX
)@@G@@      RETURN@^@@@@      ENTRY S1TIMT(I,M) @ @@@@      IF (ITEST.EQ.0) REAY
)@@G@@TURN  @#@@@@      GO TO 5     @C@@[@   10 FORMAT('0***** ELAPSED TIME ATAZ
)@@G@@ ',13A6)    @#[@@@  100 PRINT 101,I @]@@@@      RETURN@E@@@@  101 FORMATBA
)@@G@@('0VALUE OF TIME ARGUMENT OUT OF RANGE ',I10)   @]@@@@      END   ___@@@BB

)@@G@@*[@@@@*SDFF*@G@@@@      SUBROUTINE S4XTRA (DF,NVAR,NROWS,INDEX,IBASE,ISTCG
)@@G@@ATE,B,XBAR,NAME)  @F@@@@      DIMENSION INDEX(NROWS),IBASE(NROWS),ISTATECH
)@@G@@(NROWS),B(NROWS)  @B@@@@      DIMENSION XBAR(NVAR),NAME(2,NVAR)   @[@@@@CI
)@@G@@C     @G@@@@C   THIS IS A DUMMY ROUTINE. USERS CAN PROVIDE THEIR OWN VERCJ
)@@G@@SION BY     @G@@@@C   PUTTING RELOCATABLE ELEMENT IN TPF$ BEFORE EXECUTICK
)@@G@@NG PROGRAM REGAN2S@F@@@@C   OR STEPREG1S.  CALLED BY THOSE PROGRAMS AFTECL
)@@G@@R EACH GROUP OF   @G@@@@C   INDEPVAR OR BASEVAR, RESP. VARIABLES ENTERS CM
)@@G@@THE REGRESSION EQU.     @[@@@@C     @B@@@@C   DF     - NUMBER OF INPUT RCN
)@@G@@ECORDS.     @B@@@@C   NVAR   - NUMBER OF INPUT VARIABLES.   @G@@@@C   NRCO
)@@G@@OWS  - NUMBER OF VARS IN MODEL INCLUDING CONSTANT AND DEP VAR.    @G@@@@CP
)@@G@@C   INDEX  - VECTOR CONTAINING INDICES OF VARS IN MODEL.  INDEX(1)=0 FORCQ
)@@G@@@G@@@@C            CONSTANT (EVEN IF NOT COMPUTED), INDEX(NROWS)=DEP VARCR
)@@G@@ NO.  @F@@@@C   IBASE  - VECTOR GIVING GROUP NUMBERS OF VARIABLES IN MODCS
)@@G@@EL.   @G@@@@C            INDEX(1)=INDEX(NROWS)=0. OTHERWISE CONTAINS GROCT
)@@G@@UP NO. OF   @G@@@@C            BASEVAR OR INDEPVAR IND VAR. ZERO IF A FRCU
)@@G@@EEVAR VARIABLE.   @G@@@@C   ISTATE - ISTATE(I)=1 IF I-TH IND VAR IS CURRCV
)@@G@@ENTLY IN THE REGR EQU,  @G@@@@C            ELSE ZERO. ISTATE(1)=1 IF CONCW
)@@G@@STANT COMPUTED. ISTATE(NROWS) @#@@@@C            =0.  @G@@@@C   B      -CX
)@@G@@ CONTAINS REGR COEFFS. B(I) IS REGR COEFF FOR I-TH IND VAR  @G@@@@C     CY
)@@G@@       IF ISTATE(I)=1.  B(1) IS CONSTANT TERM IF ISTATE(1)=1.     @D@@@@CZ
)@@G@@C            B(NROWS) IS RESIDUAL SUM OF SQUARES.     @G@@@@C   XBAR   -DA
)@@G@@ VECTOR OF MEANS OF INPUT VARIABLES. MEAN OF I-TH IND VAR   @G@@@@C     DB
)@@G@@       IN MODEL IS XBAR(INDEX(I)). MEAN OF DEP VAR IS XBAR(INDEX  @G@@@@DC
)@@G@@C            (NROWS)).  XBAR(INDEX(1)) IS UNDEFINED SINCE INDEX(1)=0.   DD
)@@G@@@G@@@@C   NAME   - ARRAY OF NAMES.  IF NAME(1)=0 NAMES NOT AVAIL AND THIDE
)@@G@@S     @G@@@@C            ARRAY SHOULD NOT BE USED.  NAME(1,I) CONTAINS 1DF
)@@G@@ST SIX CHARS@G@@@@C            AND NAME(2,I) CONTAINS LAST TWO CHARS, LEDG
)@@G@@FT JUSTIFIED WITH @G@@@@C            IN MODEL IS NAME(1,INDEX(I)) AND NADH
)@@G@@ME(2,INDEX(I)).  NAME   @G@@@@C            FOR DEP VAR IS IN NAME(1,INDEDI
)@@G@@X(NROWS)) AND NAME(2,INDEX    @^@@@@C            (NROWS)).  @[@@@@C     DJ
)@@G@@@]@@@@      RETURN@]@@@@      END   ___@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@DK
)@@G@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@DL
)@@G@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@)@@@<@K^GK0@)@@@C@)@^@N#DM
)@@G@@^C@@@@@@@@@@/K@@@@/K@K@@@@F@@E*4@K@@@[ @@]/K@@@#N@0@@]AA@ B9)@]@K@)@A@N#DN
)@@G@@^@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@/K@@@@AA0@@#@[ ]MMS4XTRAAB@ B9DO
)@@G@@@@^@@#@@B@@[@@D@@[@@H@@[@@]@@ @C@@@C@@@@@@NERR3$      S4XTRA      @@[@@@DP
)@@G@@@@@@@A@@@@@@      ^@@@C@@]@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@DQ
)@@G@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@*[@@@@*SDFF*@G@@@@      SUBROUTINE D4XTRA (DF,NVDR
)@@G@@AR,NROWS,INDEX,IBASE,ISTATE,B,XBAR,NAME)  @ @@@@      DOUBLE PRECISION BDS
)@@G@@,XBAR @F@@@@      DIMENSION INDEX(NROWS),IBASE(NROWS),ISTATE(NROWS),B(NRDT
)@@G@@OWS)  @B@@@@      DIMENSION XBAR(NVAR),NAME(2,NVAR)   @[@@@@C     @G@@@@DU
)@@G@@C   THIS IS A DUMMY ROUTINE. USERS CAN PROVIDE THEIR OWN VERSION BY     DV
)@@G@@@G@@@@C   PUTTING RELOCATABLE ELEMENT IN TPF$ BEFORE EXECUTING PROGRAM RDW
)@@G@@EGAN2 @F@@@@C   OR STEPREG1.   CALLED BY THOSE PROGRAMS AFTER EACH GROUPDX
)@@G@@ OF   @G@@@@C   INDEPVAR OR BASEVAR, RESP. VARIABLES ENTERS THE REGRESSIDY
)@@G@@ON EQU.     @[@@@@C     @B@@@@C   DF     - NUMBER OF INPUT RECORDS.     DZ
)@@G@@@B@@@@C   NVAR   - NUMBER OF INPUT VARIABLES.   @G@@@@C   NROWS  - NUMBEEA
)@@G@@R OF VARS IN MODEL INCLUDING CONSTANT AND DEP VAR.    @G@@@@C   INDEX  -EB
)@@G@@ VECTOR CONTAINING INDICES OF VARS IN MODEL.  INDEX(1)=0 FOR@G@@@@C     EC
)@@G@@       CONSTANT (EVEN IF NOT COMPUTED), INDEX(NROWS)=DEP VAR NO.  @F@@@@ED
)@@G@@C   IBASE  - VECTOR GIVING GROUP NUMBERS OF VARIABLES IN MODEL.   @G@@@@EE
)@@G@@C            INDEX(1)=INDEX(NROWS)=0. OTHERWISE CONTAINS GROUP NO. OF   EF
)@@G@@@G@@@@C            BASEVAR OR INDEPVAR IND VAR. ZERO IF A FREEVAR VARIABEG
)@@G@@LE.   @G@@@@C   ISTATE - ISTATE(I)=1 IF I-TH IND VAR IS CURRENTLY IN THEEH
)@@G@@ REGR EQU,  @G@@@@C            ELSE ZERO. ISTATE(1)=1 IF CONSTANT COMPUTEI
)@@G@@ED. ISTATE(NROWS) @#@@@@C            =0.  @G@@@@C   B      - CONTAINS REEJ
)@@G@@GR COEFFS. B(I) IS REGR COEFF FOR I-TH IND VAR  @G@@@@C            IF ISEK
)@@G@@TATE(I)=1.  B(1) IS CONSTANT TERM IF ISTATE(1)=1.     @D@@@@C           EL
)@@G@@ B(NROWS) IS RESIDUAL SUM OF SQUARES.     @G@@@@C   XBAR   - VECTOR OF MEM
)@@G@@EANS OF INPUT VARIABLES. MEAN OF I-TH IND VAR   @G@@@@C            IN MOEN
)@@G@@DEL IS XBAR(INDEX(I)). MEAN OF DEP VAR IS XBAR(INDEX  @G@@@@C           EO
)@@G@@ (NROWS)).  XBAR(INDEX(1)) IS UNDEFINED SINCE INDEX(1)=0.   @G@@@@C   NAEP
)@@G@@ME   - ARRAY OF NAMES.  IF NAME(1)=0 NAMES NOT AVAIL AND THIS     @G@@@@EQ
)@@G@@C            ARRAY SHOULD NOT BE USED.  NAME(1,I) CONTAINS 1ST SIX CHARSER
)@@G@@@G@@@@C            AND NAME(2,I) CONTAINS LAST TWO CHARS, LEFT JUSTIFIEDES
)@@G@@ WITH @G@@@@C            IN MODEL IS NAME(1,INDEX(I)) AND NAME(2,INDEX(IET
)@@G@@)).  NAME   @G@@@@C            FOR DEP VAR IS IN NAME(1,INDEX(NROWS)) ANEU
)@@G@@D NAME(2,INDEX    @^@@@@C            (NROWS)).  @[@@@@C     @]@@@@      EV
)@@G@@RETURN@]@@@@      END   ___@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@EW
)@@G@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@EX

)@@G@@SUBROUTINE S17COR(OBS,R,KK,NOBS,VMEAN,VAR,IVAR,K)     @ @@@@      DIMENSFK
)@@G@@ION OBS(2),R(2)   @]@@@@      K=KK  @^@@@@      IF(K.GT.30) K=30  @A@@@@FL
)@@G@@      IF(K.GT.(NOBS/3)) K=NOBS/3    @#@@@@   10 DO 30 I=1,K @]@@@@      FM
)@@G@@R(I)=0@#@@@@      NNOBS=NOBS-I@^@@@@      DO 20 J=1,NNOBS   @C@@@@      FN
)@@G@@R(I)=R(I)+(OBS(J)-VMEAN)*(OBS(J+I)-VMEAN) @#@@@@   20 CONTINUE    @^@@@@FO
)@@G@@      R(I)=R(I)/VAR     @#@@@@   30 CONTINUE    @]@@@@      RETURN@]@@@@FP
)@@G@@      END   ___@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@)@@[N#[#@@K0@@@@@@G/@__-FQ

)@@G@@*[@@@@*SDFF*@G@@@@      SUBROUTINE S17NRM(NOBS,VMEAN,VAR,VMIN,VMAX,STEP,GH
)@@G@@FRCNT,NINT,PRMIN, @ @@@@     *                  PRMAX)@[@@@@C     @G@@@@GI
)@@G@@C                  SUBROUTINE TO CALCULATE EXPECTED FREQUENCY COUNTS    GJ
)@@G@@@B@@@@C                  IF VARIABLE WAS NORMAL @[@@@@C     @ @@@@      GK
)@@G@@DIMENSION FRCNT(NINT)   @^@@@@      INTEGER FRCNT     @ @@@@      DUM =(GL
)@@G@@VAR*(NOBS-1))/NOBS@^@@@@      DUM = SQRT( DUM)  @A@@@@      PR1 = PRNRM(GM
)@@G@@(VMIN-VMEAN)/DUM) @#@@@@      PRMIN = PR1 @#@@@@      FIN = VMIN  @^@@@@GN
)@@G@@      DO 20 I= 1,NINT   @^@@@@      FIN = FIN + STEP  @A@@@@      PR2 = GO
)@@G@@PRNRM((FIN-VMEAN)/DUM)  @B@@@@      FRCNT(I) = (PR2-PR1)*NOBS  +0.5     GP
)@@G@@@#@@@@      PR1 = PR2   @#@@@@   20 CONTINUE    @#@@@@      PRMAX= 1-PR2GQ
)@@G@@@]@@@@      RETURN@]@@@@      END   ___@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@GR

)@@G@@SUBROUTINE S17RMD(OBS,MEDIAN,NOBS,NRUNS,Z,NABOVE,NBELOW)    @#@@@@      HH
)@@G@@REAL MEDIAN @^@@@@      DIMENSION OBS(2)  @G@@@@C        NABOVE IS NUMBEHI
)@@G@@R OF ELEMENTS ABOVE MEDIAN,NBELOW IS NUMBER OF  @G@@@@C        ELEMENTS HJ
)@@G@@BELOW MEDIAN,NRUNS IS NUMBER OF RUNS,NOLDRN CONTAINS  @G@@@@C        INFHK
)@@G@@O ABOUT PREVIOUS ELEMENT,+1 FOR EL. ABOVE MED.,-1 FOR EL.   @^@@@@C     HL
)@@G@@   BELOW MED.     @[@@@@C     @#@@@@      NRUNS=1     @^@@@@      DO 30 HM
)@@G@@I=1,NOBS    @ @@@@      IF(OBS(I)-MEDIAN)20,30  @#@@@@      NABOVE=1    HN
)@@G@@@#@@@@      NBELOW=0    @#@@@@      NOLDRN=1    @#@@@@      IBEG=I+1    HO
)@@G@@@#@@@@      GO TO 40    @#@@@@   20 NBELOW=1    @#@@@@      NABOVE=0    HP
)@@G@@@#@@@@      NOLDRN=-1   @#@@@@      IBEG=I+1    @#@@@@      GO TO 40    HQ
)@@G@@@#@@@@   30 CONTINUE    @#@@@@      GO TO 100   @^@@@@   40 DO 90 I=IBEGHR
)@@G@@,NOBS @^@@@@      DIF=OBS(I)-MEDIAN @^@@@@      IF(DIF)50,90,60   @^@@@@HS
)@@G@@   50 NBELOW=NBELOW+1   @ @@@@      IF(NOLDRN) 90,70,70     @^@@@@   60 HT
)@@G@@NABOVE=NABOVE+1   @ @@@@      IF(NOLDRN) 70,70,90     @^@@@@   70 NRUNS=HU
)@@G@@NRUNS+1     @^@@@@      NOLDRN=-NOLDRN    @#@@@@   90 CONTINUE    @ @@@@HV
)@@G@@      IF(NOBS.LE.40) RETURN   @ @@@@      DIF=(NABOVE+NBELOW)/2   @A@@@@HW
)@@G@@      Z=(NRUNS-DIF+1)/SQRT(DIF/2)   @]@@@@  100 RETURN@]@@@@      END   HX
)@@G@@___@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@HY

)@@G@@*[@@@@*SDFF*@G@@@@      SUBROUTINE S17CPT(X,N,R,IR,DR,H,IH,DH,RUNS,HIST,LK
)@@G@@OTF,MDATA,NHIST,  @ @@[@     *VMIN1,VMAX1,FIRST,IERR) @[[@@@C     @G@@@@LL
)@@G@@C                  SUBROUTINE TO COMPUTE RUNS, HISTOGRAMS FOR A VARIABLELM
)@@G@@@G@@@@C                  HAVING N VALUES STORED IN X, R IS VECTOR CONTAILN
)@@G@@NING  @H@@@@C                  RESULTS ABOUT RUNS, H IS A VECTOR CONTAINLO
)@@G@@ING FREQUENCY     @G@@@@C                  COUNTS,IN SOME CASES ALSO MEALP
)@@G@@NS AND VARIANCES FOR A  @G@@@@C                  HISTOGRAM , R(7) IS NUMLQ
)@@G@@BER OF MISSING DATA(OUTPUT)   @[@@@@C     @G@@@@      DIMENSION R(9), H(LR
)@@G@@2), X(2), DR(4),IR(10),IUPDWN(2),IH(2),DH(2)    @B@@@@      DATA IUPDWN(LS
)@@G@@1)/2/, IUPDWN(2)/1/     @B@@@@      LOGICAL RUNS, HIST,OTF,MDATA,FIRST  LT
)@@G@@@A@@@@      DOUBLE PRECISION  DR ,DH,DWORK@^@@@@      INTEGER DNEXT     LU
)@@G@@@ @@@@      DEFINE IFN(I)=IUPDWN(I) @[@@@@C     @E@@@@C                 LV
)@@G@@ IR(1) = NUMBER OF RUNS WITH LENGTH LLRUN @H@@@@C                  R(2) LW
)@@G@@ = VALUE OF PREVIOUS OBSERVATION FOR EACH VARIABLE    @F@@@@C           LX
)@@G@@       IR(3) = LENGTH OF ACTIVE RUN FOR EACH VARIABLE @D@@@@C           LY
)@@G@@       IR(4) = LENGTH OF THE LONGEST RUN  @D@@@@C                  IR(5)LZ
)@@G@@ = CURRENT NUMBER OF TIES     @G@@@@C                  IR(6) = SWITCH (=MA
)@@G@@1 IF PREVIOUS RUN WAS RUN DOWN,     @F@@@@C                             MB
)@@G@@     =2 IF PREVIOUS RUN WAS RUN UP) @D@@@@C                  IR(7) = NUMMC
)@@G@@BER OF NON-MISSING DATA @A@@@@C                  R(8)  = VMIN     @A@@@@MD
)@@G@@C                  R(9)  = VMAX     @B@@@@C                  IR(10) = NUME
)@@G@@MBER OF RUNS@A@@@@C                  DR(1) = VMEAN    @B@@@@C           MF
)@@G@@       DR(2) = SUM OF SQUARES @B@@@@C                  DR(3) = SUM OF CUMG
)@@G@@BES   @C@@@@C                  DR(4) = SUM OF FOURTH POWERS @[@@@@C     MH
)@@G@@@]@@@@      J = N @ @@@@      IF(.NOT.OTF)  GO TO 40  @]@@@@      J = 1 MI
)@@G@@@^@@@@      DO 30 I = 1,N     @#@@@@      WORK = X(I) @ @@@@      IF(.NOMJ
)@@G@@T.MDATA) GO TO 25 @ @@@@      IF(WORK.NE.0.)  GO TO 25@B@@@@      IF(FLDMK
)@@G@@(0,1,WORK).NE.1)  GO TO 25    @^@@@@      IR(7)=IR(7)+1     @#@@@@      ML
)@@G@@GO TO 30    @A@@@@   25 IF(WORK.LT.R(8)) R(8) = WORK  @A@@@@      IF(WORMM
)@@G@@K.GT.R(9))  R(9) = WORK @ @@@@      DR(1) = DR(1) + WORK    @^@@@@      MN
)@@G@@W2 = WORK * WORK  @^@@@@      DR(2) = DR(2) + W2@A@@@@      DR(3) = DR(3MO
)@@G@@) + WORK * W2     @ @@@@      DR(4) = DR(4) + W2*W2   @#@@@@      X(J) =MP
)@@G@@ X(I) @#@@@@      J = J + 1   @#@@@@   30 CONTINUE    @#@@@@      J = J MQ
)@@G@@- 1   @ @@@@   40 IF(.NOT.RUNS)  GO TO 140@^@@@@      IF(FIRST) GO TO 45MR
)@@G@@@]@@@@      IBEG=1@#@@@@      GO TO 75    @#@@@@   45 IR(5)=0     @#@@@@MS
)@@G@@      IR(4)=0     @#@@@@      IR(3)=0     @#@@@@      IR(10)=1    @]@@@@MT
)@@G@@      J1=J-1@#@@@@      DO 70 I=1,J1@ @@@@      IF(X(I+1)-X(I)) 50,65,55MU
)@@G@@@#@@@@   50 IR(6)=1     @#@@@@      GO TO 60    @#@@@@   55 IR(6)=2     MV
)@@G@@@^@@@@   60 IR(3)=IR(5)+1     @#@@@@      IR(5)=0     @#@@@@      R(2)=XMW
)@@G@@(I+1) @#@@@@      IBEG=I+2    @ @@@@      IF(J.GT.2) GO TO 75     @#@@@@MX
)@@G@@      IR(3)=1     @#@@@@      GO TO 140   @^@@@@   65 IR(5)=IR(5)+1     MY
)@@G@@@#@@@@   70 CONTINUE    @#@@@@      GO TO 140   @^@@@@   75 DO 130 I=IBEMZ
)@@G@@G,J   @#@@@@      WORK = X(I) @#@@@@      ISW=IR(6)   @^@@@@      GO TO NA
)@@G@@(80,120),ISW@[@@@@C     @C@@@@C                  PREVIOUS RUN WAS RUN DONB
)@@G@@WN    @[@@@@C     @A@@@@   80 IF(R(2)-WORK)  85,100,110     @[@@@@C     NC
)@@G@@@E@@@@C                  NEW RUN IS DIFFERENT FROM PREVIOUS ONE   @[@@@@ND
)@@G@@C     @^@@@@   85 IR(10)=IR(10)+1   @ @@@@      IF(IR(3)-IR(4)) 98,90,95NE
)@@G@@@[@@@@C     @G@@@@C                  LENGTH OF LAST RUN WAS EQUAL TO LENNF
)@@G@@GTH OF MAX RUN    @[@@@@C     @^@@@@   90 IR(1) = IR(1) + 1 @#@@@@      NG
)@@G@@GO TO 98    @[@@@@C     @E@@@@C                  LENGTH WAS BIGGER THAN NH
)@@G@@MAXIMUM LENGTH    @[@@@@C     @^@@@@   95 IR(4) = IR(3)     @#@@@@      NI
)@@G@@IR(1) = 1   @#@@@@   98 IR(3) = 1   @#@@@@      R(2) = WORK @ @@@@      NJ
)@@G@@IF(IR(5).EQ.0)  GO TO 99@ @@@@      IR(3) = IR(3) + IR(5)   @#@@@@      NK
)@@G@@IR(5) = 0   @^@@@@   99 IR(6) = IFN(IR(6))@#@@@@      GO TO 130   @[@@@@NL
)@@G@@C     @A@@@@C                  TIE APPEARED     @[@@@@C     @^@@@@  100 NM
)@@G@@IR(5) = IR(5) + 1 @#@@@@      GO TO 130   @C@@@@C                  NEW RNN
)@@G@@UN IS SAME AS LAST RUN  @A@@@@  110 IR(3) = IR(3) + IR(5) + 1     @#@@@@NO
)@@G@@      R(2) = WORK @#@@@@      IR(5) = 0   @#@@@@      GO TO 130   @[@@@@NP
)@@G@@C     @B@@@@C                  PREVIOUS RUN WAS RUN UP@[@@@@C     @A@@@@NQ
)@@G@@  120 IF(R(2)-WORK)  110,100,85     @#@@@@  130 CONTINUE    @[@@@@C     NR
)@@G@@@G@@@@C                  END OF RUNS, COMPUTE HISTOGRAMS IF ANY SPECIFIENS
)@@G@@D     @[@@@@C     @ @@@@  140 IF(.NOT.HIST)  GO TO 180@]@@[@      IERR=0NT
)@@G@@@#@@@@      ISTART = 1  @A@@@@      IF(NHIST.EQ.0)  GO TO 180     @ @@@@NU
)@@G@@      DO 175 II = 1,NHIST     @A@@@@      NEXT = IH(ISTART) + ISTART    NV
)@@G@@@ @@@@      INDREL = ISTART + 5     @^@@@@      VMIN = H(ISTART+3)@^@@@@NW
)@@G@@      VMAX = H(ISTART+4)@C@@@@      IF(VMIN.NE.0.OR.VMAX.NE.0)  GO TO 15NX
)@@G@@0     @#@@@@      VMIN = VMIN1@#@@@@      VMAX = VMAX1@ @@@@      H(ISTANY
)@@G@@RT+3) = VMIN1     @ @@@@      H(ISTART+4) = VMAX1     @C@@@@      H(ISTANZ
)@@G@@RT+2) = (VMAX1-VMIN1)/(H(ISTART)-8) @#@@@@      GO TO 155   @^@@@@  150 OA
)@@G@@STEP = H(ISTART+2)@#@@@@  155 DO 170 I=1,J@#@@@@      WORK = X(I) @A@@@@OB
)@@G@@      IF(WORK.LT.VMIN)  GO TO 158   @ @@@@      IF(WORK-VMAX) 156,,160  OC
)@@G@@@[@@@@C     @F@@@@C                  COMPUTE ADDRESS FOR INCREASING FREQOD
)@@G@@UENCY COUNTS@[@@@@C     @B@@@@      INDEX=(WORK-VMIN)/STEP+INDREL-1     OE
)@@G@@@#@@@@      GO TO 157   @B@@@@  156 INDEX = (WORK-VMIN)/STEP + INDREL   OF
)@@G@@@A@@@@  157 IH(INDEX) = IH(INDEX) + 1     @[@@@@C     @G@@@@C           OG
)@@G@@       COMPUTE MEAN AND VARIANCE FOR NON-NODIST HISTOGRAM   @[@@@@C     OH
)@@G@@@ @@[@      IDISTR=IH(ISTART+1)     @A@@[@      IF(IDISTR.EQ.1) GO TO 17OI
)@@G@@0     @#[@@@      DNEXT=NEXT/2@A@@[@      IF(IDISTR.NE.5) GO TO 1157    OJ
)@@G@@@D@@[@      IF(DIM(WORK,AINT(WORK+0.001)).GT.1.0E-6) IERR=1 @A@@[@      OK
)@@G@@DH(DNEXT-1)=DH(DNEXT-1)+WORK  @#@@[@      GO TO 170   @#@@[@ 1157 DWORK=OL
)@@G@@WORK  @A[@@@      DH(DNEXT-1)=DH(DNEXT-1)+DWORK @B@@@@      DH(DNEXT)=DHOM
)@@G@@(DNEXT)+DWORK*DWORK     @#@@@@      GO TO 170   @[@@@@C     @F@@@@C     ON
)@@G@@             OBSERVATION WAS SMALLER THAN MINIMUM SPECIFIED @[@@@@C     OO
)@@G@@@D@@@@  158 FLD(0,18,H(NEXT-5)) = FLD(0,18,H(NEXT-5)) + 1   @#@@@@      OP
)@@G@@GO TO 170   @[@@@@C     @F@@@@C                  OBSERVATION WAS BIGGER OQ
)@@G@@THAN MAXIMUM SPECIFIED  @[@@@@C     @D@@@@  160 FLD(18,18,H(NEXT-5)) = FOR
)@@G@@LD(18,18,H(NEXT-5)) + 1 @#@@@@  170 CONTINUE    @^@@@@      ISTART = NEXOS
)@@G@@T     @#@@@@  175 CONTINUE    @]@@@@  180 RETURN@]@@@@      END   ___4) OT
)@@G@@= IR(3)     @#@@@@      IR(1) = 1   @#@@@@   98 )@@[M[#[#@K0@@@@@@G.)__"OU
)@@G@@C[)@@)R8:K@#G.@__"C[@@@ZG/)@@[C@)@@ZR8VK@]G@FK@[C/@__"AA@ B7)@E[MK0K0K0KOV

)@@G@@*[@@@@*SDFF*@D@@@@      SUBROUTINE S17PSN(NOBS,VMEAN,NINT,IFRCNT,PRMAX) RB
)@@G@@@[@@@@C     @E@@@@C        SUBROUTINE TO CALCULATE EXPECTED FREQUENCY CORC
)@@G@@UNTS  @A@@@@C        FOR POISSON DISTRIBUTION   @[@@@@C     @ @@@@      RD
)@@G@@DIMENSION IFRCNT(NINT)  @ @@@@      PR1=PRPSN(VMEAN,0.)     @^@@@@      RE
)@@G@@DO 10 I=1,NINT    @]@@@@      X=I-1 @^@@@@      PR2=PRPSN(VMEAN,X)@A@@@@RF
)@@G@@      IFRCNT(I)=(PR2-PR1)*NOBS+0.5  @#@@@@      PR1=PR2     @#@@@@   10 RG
)@@G@@CONTINUE    @#@@@@      PRMAX=1-PR1 @]@@@@      RETURN@]@@@@      END   RH
)@@G@@___@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@RI

)@@G@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@*[@@@@*SDFF*@F@@@@      SUBROUTINE S17RHI(SCR,NWRY
)@@G@@,MSTOR,FCOUNT,BASE,IBASE,NVARS,$)   @E@@@@      DIMENSION BASE(NVARS),SCRZ
)@@G@@R(NW),FCOUNT(MSTOR),IBASE(2)  @^@@@@      INTEGER CONST     @#@@@@      SA
)@@G@@COMMON X(2) @^@@@@      DATA CONST/10/    @B@@@@      CALL S1GTAG('HIST'SB
)@@G@@,IFW,NWE,NEL,$997)@^@@@@      DO 40 I=1,NVARS   @^@@@@      BASE(I)=X(IFSC
)@@G@@W)    @#@@@@   40 IFW=IFW+1   @B@@@@      IF((NVARS+NW).NE.NEL) GO TO 99SD
)@@G@@7     @#@@@@      DO 60 I=1,NW@^@@@@      SCR(I)= X(IFW)    @#@@@@   60 SE
)@@G@@IFW=IFW+1   @]@@@@      RETURN@F@@@@      ENTRY S17RHT(IVAR,FCOUNT,ICOUNSF
)@@G@@T,NHIST,VMIN,VMAX,IDIM,FIRST) @^@@@@      LOGICAL FIRST     @ @@@@      SG
)@@G@@DIMENSION ICOUNT(2)     @#@@@@      NHIST=0     @]@@@@      IDIM=0@ @@@@SH
)@@G@@      IF(.NOT.FIRST) GO TO 67 @^@@@@      DO 65 I=1,MSTOR   @#@@@@   65 SI
)@@G@@FCOUNT(I)=0 @^@@@@   67 NBEG=IBASE(IVAR)  @#@@@@      NBASE=1     @ @@@@SJ
)@@G@@   70 IF(NBEG.EQ.0) GO TO 110 @#@@@@      VMIN1=VMIN  @#@@@@      VMAX1=SK

)@@G@@SUBROUTINE S17LRN(N,IP,P1,P2) @#@@@@C     R. ST.JOHN  @I@@@@C     THIS RUT
)@@G@@OUTINE FINDS THE PROB THAT THE LONGEST RUN (GIVEN N OBS) HAS LENGTH     UU
)@@G@@@H@@@@C     IP OR LESS (P2), AND ALSO THE PROB THAT THE LONGEST RUN HAS UV
)@@G@@LENGTH IP OR@#@@@@C     MORE (P1).  @G@@@@C     FOR N.LE.21, THE EXACT PUW
)@@G@@ROBS ARE GIVEN FROM OLMSTEAD'S(AMS,1946)  @^@@@@C     TABLE(EXTENDED    UX
)@@G@@@G@@@@C     FOR N.GT.21, THE POISSON APPROX IS USED, AS GIVEN BY OLMSTEAUY
)@@G@@D     @#@@@@C     N=NO. OF OBS@B@@@@C     IP=LENGTH OF LONGEST RUN UP ANUZ
)@@G@@D DOWN@A@@@@C     P1=PR(RUN OF LENGTH .GE.IP)   @A@@@@C     P2=PR(RUN OFVA
)@@G@@ LENGTH .LE. IP)  @A@@@@      DOUBLE PRECISION ARG,GAMMAF   @ @@@@      VB
)@@G@@DIMENSION TABLE(21,4)   @ @@@@      DATA  TABLE(1,1)  /1.00/@B@@@@      VC
)@@G@@DATA (TABLE(2,I),I=1,2)/1.00,.33/   @C@@@@      DATA (TABLE(3,I),I=1,3)/VD
)@@G@@1.00,.58,.08/     @C@@@@      DATA (TABLE(4,I),I=1,4)/1.00,.73,.15,.02/ VE
)@@G@@@C@@@@      DATA (TABLE(5,I),I=1,4)/1.00,.83,.22,.03/ @C@@@@      DATA (VF
)@@G@@TABLE(6,I),I=1,4)/1.00,.89,.28,.04/ @C@@@@      DATA (TABLE(7,I),I=1,4)/VG
)@@G@@1.00,.93,.33,.06/ @C@@@@      DATA (TABLE(8,I),I=1,4)/1.00,.96,.38,.07/ VH
)@@G@@@C@@@@      DATA (TABLE(9,I),I=1,4)/1.00,.97,.43,.09/ @C@@@@      DATA (VI
)@@G@@TABLE(10,I),I=1,4)/1.00,.98,.47,.10/@C@@@@      DATA (TABLE(11,I),I=1,4)VJ
)@@G@@/1.00,.99,.51,.11/@C@@@@      DATA (TABLE(12,I),I=1,4)/1.00,.99,.55,.12/VK
)@@G@@@D@@@@      DATA (TABLE(13,I),I=1,4)/1.00,1.00,.58,.14/     @D@@@@      VL
)@@G@@DATA (TABLE(14,I),I=1,4)/1.00,1.00,.61,.15/     @D@@@@      DATA (TABLE(VM
)@@G@@15,I),I=1,4)/1.00,1.00,.64,.16/     @D@@@@      DATA (TABLE(16,I),I=1,4)VN
)@@G@@/1.00,1.00,.67,.17/     @D@@@@      DATA (TABLE(17,I),I=1,4)/1.00,1.00,.VO
)@@G@@70,.19/     @D@@@@      DATA (TABLE(18,I),I=1,4)/1.00,1.00,.72,.20/     VP
)@@G@@@D@@@@      DATA (TABLE(19,I),I=1,4)/1.00,1.00,.74,.21/     @D@@@@      VQ
)@@G@@DATA (TABLE(20,I),I=1,4)/1.00,1.00,.76,.22/     @]@@@@      P1=0.0@#@@@@VR
)@@G@@      P2=1.00     @A@@@@      IF(N.LT.2.OR.IP.LT.1)GO TO 99 @ @@@@      VS
)@@G@@IF(IP.GT.N-1)GO TO 99   @^@@@@      IF(IP.GT.15)RETURN@ @@@@      IF(N.GVT
)@@G@@T.21)GO TO 50     @ @@@@      IF(IP.GT.4)GO TO 50     @A@@@@C     DO TABVU
)@@G@@LE LOOK-UP FOR P1 AND P2@]@@@@      M=N-1 @^@@@@      P1=TABLE(M,IP)    VV
)@@G@@@ @@@@      IF(IP.EQ.4)GO TO 20     @]@@@@      J=IP+1@^@@@@      P2=1.-VW
)@@G@@TABLE(M,J)  @^@@@@      IF(M.EQ.1)P2=P1   @^@@@@      IF(IP.EQ.M)P2=1.00VX
)@@G@@@]@@@@      RETURN@#@@@@20    ARG=IP+4    @^@@@@      GAM1=GAMMAF(ARG)  VY
)@@G@@@#@@@@      GO TO 30    @#@@@@50    ARG=IP+3    @^@@@@      GAM=GAMMAF(AVZ
)@@G@@RG)   @#@@@@      ARG=IP+4    @^@@@@      GAM1=GAMMAF(ARG)  @D@@@@      WA
)@@G@@P1=1.-EXP(-2.*((N-IP)*(IP+1.)+1.)/GAM     )     @D@@@@30    P2=EXP(-2.*(WB
)@@G@@(N-IP-1.)*(IP+2.)+1.)/GAM1     )    @]@@@@      RETURN@^@@@@99    PRINT WC
)@@G@@100,N,IP    @G@@@@100   FORMAT(1H1,' UNISTAT1 ERROR*****. THE VALUES N='WD
)@@G@@,I10,' AND IP=',  @B@@@@     XI10,' ARE NOT ACCEPTABLE IN S17LRN')@]@@@@WE
)@@G@@      RETURN@]@@@@      END   ___NDS THE PROB THAT THE LONGEST RUN (GIVEWF

)@@G@@*[@@@@*SDFF*@A@@@@      SUBROUTINE S17RNS(N,IR,P1,P2) @#@@@@C      R. STYB
)@@G@@.JOHN @H@@@@C     THIS ROUTINE FINDS THE PROB OF IR OR FEWER (P2) AND IRYC
)@@G@@ OR MORE (P1) RUNS@ @@@@C     UP AND DOWN FOR N OBS.  @G@@@@C     FOR N.YD
)@@G@@LT.7,TABULATED VALUES ARE GIVEN FROM EDGINGTON (JASA,1961)  @G@@@@C    FYE
)@@G@@OR N.GE.7, THE NORMAL APPROX IS USED, AS GIVEN BY BRADLEY (P279)  @^@@@@YF
)@@G@@C     N=NO. OF OBS.     @A@@@@C     IR=NO. OF RUNS UP AND DOWN    @ @@@@YG
)@@G@@C     P1=PR(IR OR MORE RUNS)  @ @@@@C     P2=PR(IR OR FEWER RUNS) @F@@@@YH
)@@G@@C     TABLE(I,J) CONTAINS PROB OF J OR FEWER RUNS FOR I+1 OBS.    @ @@@@YI
)@@G@@      DIMENSION TABLE(5,5)    @ @@@@      DATA  TABLE(1,1) /1.00/ @B@@@@YJ
)@@G@@      DATA (TABLE(2,I),I=1,2)/.33,1.00/   @C@@@@      DATA (TABLE(3,I),IYK
)@@G@@=1,3)/.08,.58,1.00/     @C@@@@      DATA(TABLE(4,I),I=1,4)/.02,.25,.73,1YL
)@@G@@.00/  @D@@@@      DATA(TABLE(5,I),I=1,5)/.00,.09,.41,.83,1.00/    @#@@@@YM

)@@G@@SUBROUTINE S17ACP(X,N,IH,VALUE,N1,IOVER)  @[@@@@C     @F@@@@C        SUBAK
)@@G@@ROUTINE TO COMPUTE FREQUENCY COUNTS FOR ALPHANUMERIC  @G@@@@C        HISAL
)@@G@@TOGRAMS, X IS VECTOR OF OBSERVATIONS, N IS ITS DIMENSION,   @G@@@@C     AM
)@@G@@   IH IS VECTOR CONTAINING FREQUENCY COUNTS, VALUE IS VECTOR OF   @G@@@@AN
)@@G@@C        FIRST 50 LEVELS OF THE VARIABLE, N1 IS NUMBER OF ALL DIFFERENT AO
)@@G@@@^@@@@C        LEVELS FOUND   @[@@@@C     @G@@[@C        S17ACP CAN BE CAP
)@@G@@ALLED SEVERAL TIMES FOR THE SAME VARIABLE IF    @G@@[@C        ALL DATA AQ
)@@G@@VALUES DO NOT FIT IN X AT THE SAME TIME. ON THE FIRST @C@@[@C        CALAR
)@@G@@L FOR EACH VARIABLE N1 MUST BE ZERO.@[@@[@C     @A@@@@      DIMENSION X(AS
)@@G@@N),IH(2),VALUE(2) @#@@@@      IOVER=0     @]@@[@      K=1   @ @@[@      AT
)@@G@@IF(N1.GT.0) GO TO 5     @^@@[@      VALUE(1)=X(1)     @]@@[@      N1=1  AU
)@@G@@@#@@[@      IH(1)=1     @]@@[@      K=2   @^@@[@    5 IF(N.LT.K) RETURN AV
)@@G@@@#@@[@      DO 20 I=K,N @#[@@@      WORK=X(I)   @#@@@@      DO 10 J=1,N1AW
)@@G@@@A@@@@      IF(WORK.NE.VALUE(J)) GO TO 10 @^@@@@      IH(J )=IH(J )+1   AX
)@@G@@@#@@@@      GO TO 20    @#@@@@   10 CONTINUE    @ @@@@      IF(N1.GE.50)AY
)@@G@@ GO TO 15   @#@@@@      N1=N1+1     @^@@@@      VALUE(N1)=WORK    @#@@[@AZ
)@@G@@      IH(N1)=1    @#[@@@      GO TO 20    @^@@@@   15 IOVER=IOVER+1     BA
)@@G@@@#@@@@   20 CONTINUE    @]@@@@      RETURN@]@@@@      END   ___@@@@@@@@@BB

)@@G@@SUBROUTINE S22DIO(BUF,LEN,$)  @ @@@@      IMPLICIT INTEGER(A-Z)   @^@@@@FG
)@@G@@      DIMENSION BUF(LEN)@[@@@@C     @[@@@@C     @E@@@@C             CROSFH
)@@G@@TAB2 DRUM INPUT SUBROUTINE.  THIS ROUTINE @C@@@@C             IS ADAPTEDFI
)@@G@@ FROM ROUTINE S22IOD AND@C@@@@C             PROVIDES FOR INPUT FROM THE FJ
)@@G@@LARGE @C@@@@C             CROSTAB2 FILE ON UNIT S22UNIT.    @[@@@@C     FK
)@@G@@@D@@@@C             CALL TO S22DIO SPECIFIES THE BUFFER AND @A@@@@C     FL
)@@G@@        INITIALIZES COUNTERS. @[@@@@C     @C@@@@C             OTHER ENTRFM
)@@G@@Y POINTS ARE PROVIDED TO@D@@@@C             READ, REWIND, AND SET STORE FN
)@@G@@INCREMENT.  @[@@@@C     @[@@@@C     @^@@@@      DIMENSION FNAM(2) @A@@@@FO
)@@G@@      DATA FNAM /'XT2$$S      '/    @^@@@@      DIMENSION R(1)    @[@@@@FP
)@@G@@C     @[@@@@C     @[@@@@C     @A@@@@      CALL S1UNIT(FNAM,DEV,X,X,X)   FQ
)@@G@@@ @@@@      IF(DEV .LE. 0) GO TO 50 @#@@@@ 30   NS=LEN/28   @#@@@@      FR
)@@G@@TOP=NS*28   @]@@@@      P=0   @]@@@@      S=0   @]@@@@      INC=1 @]@@@@FS
)@@G@@      RETURN@#@@@@ 50   RETURN 3    @[@@@@C     @ @@@@C             REWIFT
)@@G@@ND ENTRY    @[@@@@C     @#@@@@      ENTRY S22DRW@]@@@@      P=0   @]@@@@FU
)@@G@@      S=0   @]@@@@      INC=1 @]@@@@      RETURN@[@@@@C     @B@@@@C     FV
)@@G@@        SET STORE INCREMENT ENTRY   @[@@@@C     @^@@@@      ENTRY S22DSKFW
)@@G@@(UI)  @]@@@@      INC=UI@]@@@@      RETURN@[@@@@C     @^@@@@C           FX
)@@G@@  READ ENTRY@[@@@@C     @ @@@@      ENTRY S22DRD(R,NR,$)    @ @@@@      FY
)@@G@@IF(P .NE. 0) GO TO 320  @B@@@@      CALL S1DRUM($360,FNAM,2,BUF,S,TOP)  FZ
)@@G@@@]@@@@      S=S+NS@]@@@@ 320  LI=1  @^@@@@      DO 350 I=1,NR     @]@@@@GA
)@@G@@      P=P+1 @A@@@@      IF (P .LE. TOP) GO TO 340     @B@@@@      CALL SGB
)@@G@@1DRUM($360,FNAM,2,BUF,S,TOP)  @]@@@@      S=S+NS@]@@@@      P=1   @#@@@@GC
)@@G@@ 340  R(LI)=BUF(P)@#@@@@ 350  LI=LI+INC   @]@@@@      RETURN@#@@@@ 360  GD
)@@G@@RETURN 3    @]@@@@      END   ___@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@GE
)@@G@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@)@@@K@)@@@;]]A^GCSK0--#@@[D@@J@@@@@^@@@@@^@@@@@^GF

)@@G@@SUBROUTINE S1COPI(NV,S,XMIN,XMAX,PROD,XBUF,DS,DXMIN,DXMAX,DPROD,  @A@@@@IT
)@@G@@     *DXBUF,PREC,SGLDBL,IFIRST)     @]@@[@C     SJM   @G@@[@C     TITLE IU
)@@G@@     - STORE DATA FROM INPUT CARRY-OVER PACKAGE (S1COPI)    @C@@[@C     IV
)@@G@@AUTHOR     - JANA VRABEC, DECEMBER, 1970  @F@@[@C     PROGRAMMER - J. R.IW
)@@G@@ ALLEN AND R. I. VOYTECKI, AUGUST, 1969   @[@@[@C     @#@@[@C 1.0 PURPOSIX
)@@G@@E     @G@@[@C     S1COPI AND S1COPS ARE USED TO STORE DATA FROM AN INPUTIY
)@@G@@ CARRY-OVER @G@@[@C     PACKAGE.  S1COPI IS THE INITIALIZATION ENTRY POIIZ
)@@G@@NT.  S1COPS IS    @G@@[@C     CALLED TO STORE DATA FROM ONE CARD IMAGE. JA
)@@G@@ FIRST NV VALUES ARE PUT@F@@[@C     INTO S(DS), NEXT NV VALUES INTO XMINJB
)@@G@@(DXMIN), NV VALUES INTO @G@@[@C     XMAX(DXMAX) AND LAST NV*(NV+1)/2 VALJC
)@@G@@UES INTO PROD(DPROD).  VALUES @G@@[@C     CAN BE CONVERTED FROM SINGLE TJD
)@@G@@O DOUBLE OF FROM DOUBLE TO SINGLE.  @[@@[@C     @^@@[@C 2.0 CALLING SEQUJE
)@@G@@ENCE  @E@@[@C 2.1 ENTRY S1COPI IS CALLED WITH A STATEMENT OF THE FORM   JF
)@@G@@@G@@[@C        CALL S1COPI(NV,S,XMIN,XMAX,PROD,XBUF,DS,DXMIN,DXMAX,DPRODJG
)@@G@@,     @C@@[@C                   DXBUF,PREC,SGLDBL,IFIRST)   @]@@[@C     JH
)@@G@@WHERE @B@@[@C     NV      IS THE NUMBER OF VARIABLES  @G@@[@C     S     JI
)@@G@@  VECTOR WHERE THE SUMS ARE TO BE STORED (IN CASES S-TO-S OR@^@@[@C     JJ
)@@G@@        D-TO-S)   @G@@[@C     XMIN    VECTOR WHERE MINIMUM VALUES ARE TOJK
)@@G@@ BE STORED (WHEN S-TO-S @^@@[@C             OR D-TO-S)@G@@[@C     XMAX  JL
)@@G@@  VECTOR WHERE MAXIMUM VALUES ARE TO BE STORED (WHEN S-TO-S @^@@[@C     JM
)@@G@@        OR D-TO-S)@G@@[@C     PROD    VECTOR WHERE PRODUCTS ARE TO BE STJN
)@@G@@ORED (WHEN S-TO-S OR    @^@@[@C             D-TO-S)   @G@@[@C     XBUF  JO
)@@G@@  INPUT VECTOR WITH 10 VALUES (USED WHEN S-TO-S OR S-TO-D)  @G@@[@C     JP
)@@G@@DS      VECTOR WHERE SUMS ARE TO BE STORED (WHEN D-TO-D OR S-TO-D)@G@@[@JQ
)@@G@@C     DXMIN   VECTOR WHERE MINIMUM VALUES ARE TO BE STORED (WHEN D-TO-D JR
)@@G@@@^@@[@C             OR S-TO-D)@G@@[@C     DXMAX   VECTOR WHERE MAXIMUM VJS
)@@G@@ALUES ARE TO BE STORED (WHEN D-TO-D @^@@[@C             OR S-TO-D)@G@@[@JT
)@@G@@C     DPROD   VECTOR WHERE PRODUCTS ARE TO BE STORED (WHEN D-TO-D OR    JU
)@@G@@@^@@[@C             S-TO-D)   @G@@[@C     DXBUF   INPUT VECTOR WITH 5 VAJV
)@@G@@LUES (USED WHEN D-TO-D OR D-TO-S)   @H@@[@C     PREC    HAS TWO POSSIBLEJW
)@@G@@ VALUES.  'SINGLE' DENOTES OUTPUT SHOULD BE     @G@@[@C             OF TJX
)@@G@@YPE SINGLE, 'DOUBLE' DENOTES OUTPUT OF TYPE DOUBLE.   @H@@[@C     SGLDBLJY
)@@G@@  HAS TWO POSSIBLE VALUES.  'SINGLE' DENOTES THAT INPUT IS OF     @G@@[@JZ
)@@G@@C             TYPE SINGLE AND 'DOUBLE' THAT INPUT IS OF TYPE DOUBLE.    KA
)@@G@@@G@@[@C     IFIRST  .NE.0 CAUSES THAT S,PROD,DS AND DPROD ARE SET TO ZERKB
)@@G@@O,    @G@@[@C             XMAX,XMIN,DXMAX AND DXMIN ARE SET TO LOW AND HKC
)@@G@@IGH VALUES, @G@@[@C             RESPECTIVELY.  IFIRST=0 DOES NOT INITIALKD
)@@G@@IZE THESE VALUES. @E@@[@C 2.2 ENTRY S1COPS IS CALLED WITH A STATEMENT OFKE
)@@G@@ THE FORM   @ @@[@C        CALL S1COPS(IERR)    @]@@[@C     WHERE @F@@[@KF
)@@G@@C     IERR IS THE NUMBER OF ERRORS FOUND WHILE PROCESSING DATA.   @[@@[@KG
)@@G@@C     @ @@[@C 3.0 NOTES/RELATIONSHIPS     @B@@[@C     REFERENCES TO TAGGKH
)@@G@@ED STORAGE - NONE.@ @@[@C     ROUTINES CALLED - NONE. @G@@[@C     S1COPIKI
)@@G@@ AND S1COPS ARE CALLED BY S1RCOP.  S1COPI IS CALLED ONCE FOR@G@@[@C     KJ
)@@G@@EACH INPUT COP.  S1COPS IS CALLED ONCE FOR EACH CARD IMAGE IN AN  @G@@[@KK
)@@G@@C     INPUT COP.  TWO OR MORE CARRY-OVER PACKAGES OF THE SAME SIZE CAN  KL
)@@G@@@G@@[@C     BE COMBINED BY SETTING IFIRST.EQ.0 ON ALL BUT THE FIRST CALLKM
)@@G@@ TO   @#@@[@C     S1COPI.     @[@@[@C     @]@@[@C     ENDSJM@G@@@@C FIRSKN
)@@G@@T CALL IS MADE TO ENTRY POINT S1COPI, WHICH INITIALIZES, SUBSEQUEN@G@@@@KO
)@@G@@C T CALLS ARE MADE TO S1COPS TO STORE ONE RECORD(5 OR 10 VALUES) IN S,  KP
)@@G@@@G@@@@C XMIN, XMAX, OR PROD. IF IFIRST .NE. 0, S1COPI WILL RESET S AND PKQ
)@@G@@RODTO @G@@@@C ZERO AND XMIN AND XMAX TO HIGH AND LOW VALUES. ALSO, IT SEKR
)@@G@@TS KTYPE=   @F@@@@C 1,2,3, OR 4,IF OPERATION IS SINGLE TO SINGLE, SINGLEKS
)@@G@@ TO DOUBLE, @G@@@@C DOUBLE TO SINGLE, OR DOUBLE TO DOUBLE, RESPECTIVELY.KT
)@@G@@ ALSO INITIALIZES @G@@@@C CONTROL VARIABLES ISTOP(1)-ISTOP(4), KSTOP, ANKU
)@@G@@D K, WHICH ARE USED TO  @F@@@@C DETERMINE WHICH VECTOR (S, XMIN, XMAX, PKV
)@@G@@ROD) IS BEING FILLED AND@B@@@@C WHAT LOCATION (K) WITHIN THAT VECTOR.   KW
)@@G@@@[@@@@C     @D]@@@      DIMENSION S(2),XMIN(2),XMAX(2),PROD(2),XBUF(10) KX
)@@G@@@E@@@@      DIMENSION DS(2),DXMIN(2),DXMAX(2),DPROD(2),DXBUF(2)   @E@@@@KY
)@@G@@      DOUBLE PRECISION DS,DXMAX,DXMIN,DPROD,DXBUF,DXLO,DXHI @C@@@@      KZ
)@@G@@DIMENSION  ISTOP(4),DUMHI(2),DUMLO(2)     @F@@@@      EQUIVALENCE (XHI,DLA
)@@G@@XHI),(XLO,DXLO),(DUMHI,XHI),(DUMLO,XLO)   @A@@@@      DATA DUMLO/O400000LB
)@@G@@000000,0/   @C@@@@      DATA DUMHI/O377777777777,O777777777777/   @[@@@@LC
)@@G@@C     @C@@@@      DIMENSION  OMAX(2), OMIN(2), OBLANK(2)    @C@@@@      LD
)@@G@@DATA  OMIN / O160040000000,O000000000000 /@D@@@@      DATA  OMAX / O2177LE
)@@G@@77777777, O700000000000 /     @D@@@@      DATA  OBLANK / O050505050505, LF
)@@G@@O050505050505/    @C@@@@      DOUBLE PRECISION  DMAXSL, DMINSL, DBLANK  LG
)@@G@@@G@@@@      EQUIVALENCE  ( OMAX, DMAXSL),  ( OMIN, DMINSL), ( OBLANK, DBLH
)@@G@@LANK) @[@@@@C     @[@@@@C     @ @@@@C INITIALIZE CONTROL VARIABLES@#@@@@LI
)@@G@@      ISTOP(1)=NV @#@@@@      ISTOP(2)=NV @#@@@@      ISTOP(3)=NV @ @@@@LJ
)@@G@@      ISTOP(4)=(NV*(NV+1))/2  @#@@@@      NCZ=ISTOP(4)@#@@@@      KSTOP=LK
)@@G@@1     @]@@@@      K=0   @ @@@@C DETERMINE TYPE OF PROCESSING@B@@@@      LL
)@@G@@IF (SGLDBL.EQ.'SINGLE') GO TO 1     @B@@@@      IF (SGLDBL.EQ.'DOUBLE') LM
)@@G@@GO TO 5     @#@@@@      GO TO 9999  @#@@@@    1 NELE=10     @A@@@@      LN
)@@G@@IF (PREC.EQ.'SINGLE') GO TO 10@A@@@@      IF (PREC.EQ.'DOUBLE') GO TO 20LO
)@@G@@@#@@@@      GO TO 9999  @]@@@@    5 NELE=5@A@@@@      IF (PREC.EQ.'SINGLLP
)@@G@@E') GO TO 30@A@@@@      IF (PREC.EQ.'DOUBLE') GO TO 40@#@@@@      GO TO LQ

)@@G@@2     @#@@@@      GO TO 45    @#@@@@   30 KTYPE=3     @#@@@@      PRINT LS
)@@G@@9000  @#@@@@      GO TO 45    @#@@@@   40 KTYPE=4     @B@@@@C INTTIALIZELT
)@@G@@ STORAGE AREAS IF IFIRST.NE.0 @A@@@@   45 IF (IFIRST.EQ.0) GO TO 1000   LU
)@@G@@@A@@@@      GO TO (50,70,50,70),KTYPE     @#@@@@   50 DO 55 I=1,NV@#@@@@LV
)@@G@@      S(I)=0.     @#@@@@      XMIN(I)=XHI @#@@@@   55 XMAX(I)=XLO @^@@@@LW

)@@G@@@#@@@@   70 DO 75 I=1,NV@#@@@@      DS(I)=0.D   @^@@@@      DXMIN(I)=DXHLY
)@@G@@I     @^@@@@   75 DXMAX(I)=DXLO     @^@@@@      DO 80  I=1,NCZ    @#@@@@LZ
)@@G@@   80 DPROD(I)=0.D@#@@@@      GO TO 1000  @D@@@@C ENTRY POINT TO STORE OMA
)@@G@@NE RECORD (5 OR 10 VALUES)    @ @@@@      ENTRY S1COPS( IERR)     @]@@@@MB
)@@G@@      IERR=0@C@@@@C LOOP ON NUMBER OF VALUES IN RECORD (5 OR 10)  @^@@@@MC

)@@G@@      IF( DXBUF(I) .EQ. DBLANK) GO TO 90  @A@@@@      IF (DXBUF(I).EQ.0.ME
)@@G@@0) GO TO 90 @G@@@@      IF( ABS(DXBUF(I)) .LE. DMAXSL  .AND.  ABS(DXBUF(MF
)@@G@@I)) .GE. DMINSL)  @G@@@@     2                                          MG

)@@G@@.4) GO TO 9999    @B@@@@      IF (K.LE.ISTOP(KSTOP)) GO TO 95     @^@@@@MJ
)@@G@@      KSTOP=KSTOP+1     @]@@@@      K=0   @ @@@@      IF (I.EQ.1) GO TO MK
)@@G@@90    @#@@@@      GO TO 1000  @A@@@@   95 GO TO (100,200,300,400),KSTOP ML
)@@G@@@^@@@@C STORE SUM IF KSTOP=1  @A@@@@  100 GO TO (110,120,130,140),KTYPE MM
)@@G@@@^@@@@  110 S(K)=S(K)+XBUF(I) @#@@@@      GO TO 500   @ @@@@  120 DS(K)=MN
)@@G@@DS(K)+XBUF(I)     @#@@@@      GO TO 500   @^@@@@  130 S(K)=S(K)+DXBUF(I)MO

)@@G@@(I)   @C@@@@      IF ( DXBUF(I) .EQ. DBLANK) XMIN(K) = 6H   @#@@@@      MU
